US Government and Senate Pay Attention to the Future of the Philippines 35

Roosevelt Urgently Calls for Philippine Governor for Consultation

Senate Investigation Team Returns Home via Europe

(Rome) US Senator Macado stated here today in a special interview with the Associated Press reporter, saying, "I am very happy that Japan has abolished the Washington Treaty, because when necessary, we can freely build the world's largest navy. I have always opposed the Washington Treaty." Senator Macado is one of the Senate Philippine Investigation Team and has been investigating in the Philippines for six weeks. He arrived here this morning by plane from Singapore. His words are quite meaningful. (23rd National Telegram)

(Manila) Philippine Governor Murphy has departed for the United States this afternoon due to President Roosevelt's urgent call in order to discuss the Philippine issue, and is expected to return in about three months. (23rd Reuters Dispatch)

(Washington) Senator King announced today that he intends to vigorously promote the passage of two cases, namely, requesting Congress to investigate Japan's defense projects on the mandated islands in the Pacific and whether Japan's policy towards "Manchukuo" violates the Nine-Power Treaty. King said that Japan now wants to dominate the Far East and exclude Western countries, saying, "Japan's intention to control China and the Far East is very obvious. Japan's policy towards China disregards the Nine-Power Treaty and is well known. I believe that Japan's attitude is not only related to peace in the Pacific, but also to world peace. However, I still hope that Japan can promote friendly relations and not cause other countries to suspect that Japan intends to occupy the Far East. I regret Japan's adoption of an imperialist military policy." As for the issue of Philippine independence, King said that no matter what Japan's attitude is, I really support the complete independence of the Philippines, and at the same time stipulate preferential tariffs for the Philippines. (22nd National Telegram)

Japanese Naval Representative Yamamoto Returns Home Next Week 36

Opposes Postponement of Formal Conference

Issues Declaration Before Departure

(London) Japanese Chief Expert on Naval Talks, Rear Admiral Isoroku Yamamoto, will leave here and return home no later than Tuesday next week. Before his departure, he issued a declaration, saying that the naval conference stipulated in the London and Washington Naval Treaties must be held as soon as possible within the shortest period of time. This is Japan's wish. I originally intended to return home via the United States, but now I have changed my itinerary and returned home via Siberia due to government orders to rush back to the country. If the Japanese government does not want the naval conference to be held as soon as possible, then I expect that it will never order me to rush back to the country. Therefore, I believe that even if someone proposes to postpone the naval conference to 1936, Japan will not accept it. Another expert member of the Japanese delegation, Colonel Iwashita, is scheduled to return home via the United States tomorrow. However, Japanese sources in London claim that Iwashita's trip to the United States is only a social matter, and Iwashita will not hold any formal negotiations in the United States. (22nd Havas Dispatch)

Second Day of Diet Interpellations Intensifies 37

Trampling on Human Rights, Pursuing the Responsibility of the Minister of Justice

Problems with Discipline, Yamaguchi Forces Togi to Act

(Tokyo) The Seiyukai's strategy was that on the second day, Yamaguchi Giichi took the stage in the House of Representatives to question the human rights issue, Takahashi Kumajiro questioned the rural issue, and Iwasaki Koji郎 questioned the ideological education and social policy issue. In short, this meeting is only a preliminary battle, and its main force should be poured into the budget general meeting, because it wants to determine the outcome in the budget deliberations, so it recognizes the trend of the bomb motion. Judging from the atmosphere on the first day, optimism can be held for lack of understanding. (23rd Den-tsu Telegram)

(Tokyo) Today's plenary session of the House of Peers opened at 10:16 am and immediately entered the agenda, continuing to question the ministers of state. Dr. Minobe, who does not belong to any party, took the stage to discuss the Constitution and questioned Minister of Justice Ohara on the issue of trampling on human rights, saying that the Ministry of Justice abused its power when investigating the Teijin incident and trampled on the law, which is appalling. If based on the principles of human rights and freedom under the Constitution, if there are facts such as illegal detention and torture, it constitutes a crime by the prosecutor. He then stated that during the Teijin incident, whether there were illegal arrests, detentions, and illegal investigations as rumored, and if so, it would constitute malfeasance by judicial officers, so he would like to hear the government's views. Later, he included a discussion of the facts and read aloud Mr. Shimada's diary in prison, exposing the fact that leather handcuffs were used during torture. Minister of Justice Ohara then took the stage to answer, denying that the prosecutor's office had taken improper measures, and said that there were no facts of prosecutors illegally detaining people. As for the detention issue, he said that he would reply after investigation. He further stated that if the facts as stated by the doctor were found, the persons involved would be severely punished. Finally, Dr. Minobe questioned on the spot, and the meeting adjourned at 0:05 am. (23rd Den-tsu Telegram)

(Tokyo) Dr. Minobe raised the issue of trampling on human rights in the House of Peers today, attacking the illegal actions of the prosecutor's office from a legal standpoint and pursuing the responsibility of Minister of Justice Ohara. There is still a possibility of publication on this issue. Dr. Iwata Chuzo in the House of Peers and Sanji Tadashi, the central figure in this case, in the House of Representatives, are still questioning. How the future will be is attracting much attention from all parties. (23rd Nippon News Alliance Telegram)

(Tokyo) The House of Representatives meeting opened at 1:15 pm on the 23rd. The situation was very lively with more people in the gallery than the designated number. Today, the ministers of state continued to be questioned regarding their speeches. First, Mr. Yamaguchi Giichi took the stage amidst cheers, saying that he had to raise questions about the issue of discipline of the current cabinet. The statement was then made as follows:

The previous Saito cabinet collapsed due to the issue of discipline, and the current cabinet has also experienced a similar collapse. Investigating this matter is quite related to the prestige of the country, so I will now question the issue of discipline. According to rumors, the Okada cabinet has already reviewed the qualities and character of the people entering the cabinet in advance, but there are still some cabinet members with question marks, and the Okada cabinet should bear a double responsibility for this. I am now asking Minister Togi the following questions:

When Mr. Togi traveled to China in the autumn of Showa 3, he expressed different views on the administration and China policy and issued a statement. At that time, the Tanaka cabinet adopted a tough policy towards China, and Zhang Xueliang incited an anti-Japanese movement at this time. If Mr. Togi had the same opinion as the Tanaka cabinet at that time, he would not have met with Zhang Xueliang. Mr. Togi's actions at that time were at least an agreement to ease Japan's tough policy towards China.

Minister Togi replied as follows:

I express my gratitude for Mr. Yamaguchi's intimacy, but his remarks are mostly hypothetical. My trip to China was indeed in December of Showa 3. Because many pending issues between the two countries were delayed at that time, I made this trip from South China to Shenyang for on-the-spot observation, and met with Zhang Xueliang. After returning to China, the opinions I expressed were to request recognition of the Nanjing government and withdraw the troops from Jinan. The above claims were discussed with the Tanaka cabinet and were agreed to. My opinions can be said to have been exhausted for the sake of my country, and I still believe in them. With this loyalty to the emperor and patriotism, how can I be tempted by money? In general, you can only comment after knowing what kind of person he is. Please do not speak recklessly. As for the matter of the Youth Officers' Association issuing any printed materials, I have heard of it but have not seen it. I don't need to be an opponent of those who hide their names. If anyone is my opponent, please state your name and come, and I hope that those who come will be prepared in advance. This matter was exposed since the establishment of the Inukai cabinet. I really don't want to defend it. Even if it is clarified or not, those who believe will believe it, and those who do not believe will still not believe it. Mr. Yamaguchi's so-called other rumors are not included. I hope you will not be polite and publish as much as possible. As for the various rumors of confusion and nonsense, please do not bring them to the parliament.

After Minister Togi gave the above earnest teachings and stepped down leisurely amidst the cheers of the Minsei Party, Mr. Yamaguchi immediately took the stage again to add the following arguments:

The person who issued the printed materials is an official of the Ministry of the Army, an army major. Therefore, in order to show integrity, it should be requested to cancel it, or sue for defamation, otherwise the doubts of the people cannot be eliminated.

Minister Togi replied as follows:

I have already said everything in my reply just now. The means of expressing innocence, or should be as Mr. Yamaguchi talked about, is also unknown. But whether to take it is my freedom.

Next, Mr. Takahashi Kumajiro questioned Minister of Interior Goto and Minister of the Army Hayashi, focusing on the problem of rural relief. (23rd Nippon News Agency Telegram

(Tokyo) Councillor Yamaguchi Giichi's sharp questions were unexpectedly overwhelmed by Minister Togi. However, it is heard that the reason why Mr. Yamaguchi raised this issue to deal with Mr. Togi was actually a purge within the Seiyukai. Some said that it was a deliberate challenge to the Togi faction, and others said that it instigated the military to create a rift with Mr. Togi. Various rumors are currently circulating, and it seems that there are many secrets, which is attracting much attention from the general public. (23rd Reuters Dispatch)

Japanese Propaganda to Italy 38

Says the Far Eastern Market Has a Wide Range

Italy Has Plenty of Room to Develop Trade

(Rome) Japanese Ambassador to Italy Sugimura recently issued a declaration to the "Lecture Forum" reporter, stating the mutual relations between Italy and Japan in Africa and the Far East, saying that the rumor that Abyssinia has hired Japanese military instructors is false and completely inaccurate. As for the saying that Japan is developing economically in Abyssinia, most of it is that Jews in Kobe buy Japanese goods and transport them to the capital of Abyssinia, and Japanese goods are not directly imported into Abyssinia. Mentioning the Far East, Sugimura said that I believe that Italy can develop its trade in the Far East and will not be involved with Japan at all, because the Far Eastern market is very large and there is plenty of room for development. However, in order to develop trade, the most important thing is to make the people of the Far East gain peace and tranquility. Japan's policy is aimed at this, and the result will surely satisfy all countries. Finally, the Japanese ambassador distributed samples of Japanese goods for experts to study, and said that if Japan can sign reciprocal tax regulations with Italy and import wine from Italy, it would be a great pleasure. (22nd Havas Dispatch)

US Senate Secret Vote Approves Joining the World Court 41

Condition is Non-Interference in Other Countries' Internal Affairs

Isolation Policy of Past Years Will Change

(Washington) Regarding the United States' participation in the Hague World Court, government leaders held a secret vote in the Senate, and the result was 60 people in favor, which is more than a two-thirds majority. (22nd National Telegram)

The Senate leaders discussed at today's meeting the reservation conditions regarding the United States' participation in the International Court of Justice proposed by the Senate Foreign Relations Committee. The debate was quite intense, and the vote finally decided to adopt it. This security case stipulates that the United States' participation in the International Court of Justice does not involve the internal affairs of other countries, nor does it abandon the United States' absolute power to handle purely internal affairs. The Senate leaders' actions today were due to President Roosevelt's consultation with Congress to approve the United States' participation in the International Court of Justice for the benefit of peace. The isolation policy that the United States has adhered to for more than ten years will change from now on. (22nd Reuters Dispatch)

Truth About the Massacre in French Somaliland 52

French Officer Volunteered Result

(Paris) Details continue to emerge in the past 24 hours regarding the annihilation of French officer Perenna and others by the Somali between the French Somaliland and Abyssinian border. Perenna, only 25 years old, was leading 106 soldiers on patrol near Lake Abbe when he suddenly heard fighting nearby. It turned out that several members of the Asaimaras tribe had crossed the border to attack a squad of soldiers from the Issa tribe of Somalia. The Issa soldiers were gradually losing ground due to being outnumbered. Regardless of the danger, Perenna decided to assist the Issa tribe. Upon arriving at the battlefield, he saw that his troops were far outnumbered by the enemy, as there were at least 800 Asaimaras. Perenna and his men did not retreat and opened fire to join the battle. Although the enemy's attack was fierce, Perenna and his men defended bravely. After two hours, their ammunition gradually ran out. At this point, they could have retreated and saved many, but Perenna and his men refused to show weakness and engaged the enemy in hand-to-hand combat, knowing full well that they were unlikely to defeat them. Perenna led from the front and was therefore the first to be killed. The remaining soldiers were then annihilated. Ten of them died from head injuries. Upon hearing the alarm, the Djibouti government urgently dispatched a large number of police to the southwest border to surround and arrest the enemy. People in Paris praised Perenna's bravery. Colonial Minister Roland yesterday proposed awarding him the Cross of Honor. The government has already issued an order praising Perenna's bravery. However, one senior official said that Perenna's expedition to the battlefield with a small force was not prudent. The political circles see the Asaimaras' attack as an affair between two tribes. The French government has decided not to negotiate this matter with the Abyssinian government, as the Abyssinian government cannot be held responsible for these scattered bandit groups causing trouble within Ethiopian territory. (Reuters, 20th)

(Paris) A foreign ministry spokesman declared today that France does not intend to lodge a formal protest with Abyssinia or the League of Nations regarding the massacre of one French officer, 18 soldiers, and 88 Somalis by nomadic tribes in Abyssinia. The foreign ministry most likely believes that this matter is purely an act of banditry and has no political nature. The responsible culprits are not under the jurisdiction of the Abyssinian King but belong to the Asaimara tribe, who are nomadic along the border between Abyssinia and French Somaliland and have uncertain whereabouts. Previous reports stated that France would protest to Abyssinia, demanding compensation and assurances that there would be no further intrusions into French territory. (National Telegram, 23rd)

(Paris) Previous reports that French government official named Bonard and 16 soldiers and native followers were annihilated by rebel barbarians in French Somaliland near the Abyssinian border have now been confirmed. Today, the Abyssinian Deputy Consul in Paris met with reporters from Jianqiang Bao and stated that the rebels most likely belong to the Issa tribe. The Issa tribe has been causing trouble for many years and has put the region under great pressure. They are unpredictable and difficult to pacify. The disturbance caused by natives on the Italian colonial border last month was likely caused by the same tribe. They do not have firearms, and the weapons they usually use are broad-bladed knives about 20 inches long. They also use these weapons to annihilate their enemies, but they are erratic, and it is often impossible to track them down after the fact. (National Telegram, 22nd)

French Government Plans to Issue New Treasury Bills 53

Totaling 50 Billion Francs

Bill Submitted to Parliament

(Paris) The cabinet today submitted a financial bill stipulating that the issuance of short-term treasury bonds be increased from 100 billion francs to 150 billion francs. The bill explains that this measure is not a disguised policy of currency inflation but merely to facilitate financial operations so that the state and all economic sectors can benefit. Currently, the national treasury must not only bear the usual expenses but also various social and economic bills and special national defense expenses. Due to the recent economic panic and reduced tax revenue, it has become necessary to increase the issuance of national treasury bonds to provide funding. As for issuing long-term bonds, it is particularly difficult at present, as French savers are willing to buy short-term bonds due to the unstable financial situation but demand high interest rates for long-term bonds, which would hinder economic recovery. Therefore, after careful consideration, the government decided to increase the issuance of short-term bonds. Not only that, short-term bondholders can easily discount and exchange them when they need cash, which is the same method used in the United Kingdom. This bill is valid until 1935, and the amount of issuance will be reduced by the end of this year. In short, the government maintains currency stability while allowing the national treasury to circulate cash in the market. This is the purpose of the financial bill. (Havas, 22nd)

Conclusive Evidence Against Hauptmann in Lindbergh Kidnapping Case 54

Wooden Ladder as Material Evidence

Flemington: Defense lawyers in the Lindbergh kidnapping case claimed that the wooden ladder was unrelated to the defendant and could not be considered evidence. However, the prosecutors refuted this. Today, the court ruled that the ladder could be used as material evidence. It is heard that the prosecutors will present an argument that the defendant carried Lindbergh Jr. away while he was asleep. When he was descending the ladder, the defendant lost his footing and fell, and little Lindbergh was crushed to death. The prosecutors will also prove that the ladder is the same object that a witness saw near the Lindbergh home before the kidnapping. The prosecutors are confident that a verdict can be reached within a few days. The evidence against Hauptmann in the Lindbergh kidnapping and murder is conclusive. The ransom notes were written by Hauptmann, and Hauptmann received the $50,000 ransom. These two points are undeniable. Public interest in this case remains undiminished. Many people attend the court hearings every day, and news reporters record all the details of the case in detail. (Reuters, 22nd)

Nature of the Huai River Conservancy Committee's Loan from Sassoon Bank 72

(Nanjing) Regarding the 4 million yuan loan established between the Huai River Conservancy Committee and Sassoon Bank in Shanghai, the person in charge of the committee stated that the contract signed with Sassoon cannot be called a loan, and the amount is not large. According to what he knows, it is only over one million yuan (the exact amount is unknown because the person in charge is in Shanghai and has not returned). The loan borrowed from the British Boxer Indemnity Fund by the committee is the price of materials used to purchase materials from London. Because they need cash, they negotiated with Sassoon to exchange for cash, and the bank exchanged materials from London at the price. In other words, the material cost of the loan borrowed by the Huai River Conservancy Committee from the British Boxer Indemnity Fund was paid to the Huai River Conservancy Committee by Sassoon, and Sassoon purchased the goods from London. This is an exchange procedure that is convenient for both parties and is different from a pledge. As for the use of cash, it will be used to complete the three-gate project in Huaiyin Shaobo and other places, and the Sanhong Gate project fee will be started. It is near Hongze Lake. Therefore, the four gates are related to the storage and discharge of water from the Huai River, which is used to irrigate farmland, so that all of them will be completed within two years, and will not be used for other purposes. Last Year's Aquatic Products Import Statistics 76

(Nanjing) According to the Ministry of Industries' investigation, the value of aquatic products imported last year exceeded 20 million yuan. Among them, the import of dried seafood reached over 61,480 dan. China's production of seafood was limited to just over ten varieties, such as dried mussels and scallops, with a total production of over 3,200 dan last year. The amount of imported goods exceeded domestic production by tenfold. (Special dispatch, 23rd)

International Commercial Telegraph

[A Reuters Commercial Dispatch, January 23]

Gold and Silver 118

London Gold Price: The London gold price today was 142 shillings and 1.5 pence, up half a penny.

London Silver: In the London silver market, speculators have resumed buying, while India has sold, but trading is minimal. The spot price is 24.625 pence, and the futures price is 24.75 pence, both the same as yesterday.

Exchange Rates 119

British-American: In the London foreign exchange market, fluctuations were minimal and market conditions remained quiet. The opening price for British-American exchange was $4.881875, which was 1875 lower than yesterday's closing price. At 11:00 AM, it rose by 25 to $4.884375, and in the afternoon it fell by 125 to $4.883125. At 2:00 PM, the price was $4.886875, up another 375.

British-French: The opening price was 74 francs 28, up seven pounds. By 2:00 PM in the afternoon, it had risen another six pounds to 74 francs 34.

Cotton and Wheat 120

American Cotton: The weather in the cotton-growing areas is extremely cold, which can eliminate boll weevils and lay a good foundation for new cotton crops. However, cotton prices are lower. Liverpool sold, and the decline was even worse. However, as market prices fell, some assistance came from Europe.

British Cotton: In the Liverpool cotton market, the May futures price was 6.82 at 1:00 PM today, down one pound.

British Wheat: In the Liverpool wheat market, the May futures price was 5 shillings, 1 penny, and 125, up 25.

American Wheat: The wheat market was also affected by weather news. The opening price was better than expected.

Rubber 121

London: The London rubber market was quiet this morning. The trading price for April-June futures at noon was 6.5 pence, the same as yesterday.

New York: The price of rubber for March fell six pounds, dropping below the price of 13 cents. There were few transactions and little interest. The decline at the opening this morning was mostly due to the lower prices in the London market.

Securities 122

New York: The securities market this morning remained sluggish and lacked excitement. It is expected that price fluctuations will be small and staggered. Market conditions seem lifeless, with no real upward or downward trend. Transactions are small and prices change very little. The news of increased work in steel mills was welcomed, and other business news, such as the increase in weekly electricity and oil output, also had a positive impact. However, market conditions are floating and have no direction, waiting to be pushed. The outlook is bearish at the moment.

There are currently various uncertain situations, so the market does not seem to be improving.

And Jardine Matheson & Co. reports: Before the opening of the New York stock market, the factors favorable to the market situation are (1) there is still investment demand with selective qualities in the securities market, (2) the floor is gradually becoming stronger, (3) the average daily output of oil in the past week was 2,521,000 barrels, (4) the electricity output last week was 1,778,000,000 kilowatt-hours, an increase of 9.4% compared to last year, (5) The Iron Age newspaper estimates that steel bar production last week accounted for 51.1% of production capacity, and said that although steel scrap prices have fallen, making people cautious, steel bar production is expected to increase, as the demand from the automotive industry has not shown any signs of decreasing. The factors that are unfavorable to the market situation are that the outlook for business is now quite chaotic and uncertain. If there is no external assistance, the securities market may not see prices rise again. The various market prices of New York securities are listed on the left.

The Chahar Eastern Incident Has Eased 125

The Longliang Area is Still Defended by Local Militias

Yue Kaixian Talks with Zhang and Matsui

A dispatch from Beiping states that the Japanese army's active deployment in Jehol Western has not been a matter of just one day. However, they have only been accumulating grass and storing food, and increasing troop deployment, which has been purely preparatory work, with no obvious signs of advancement. It was not until the middle of this month that they gradually became active, claiming that the Longliang, Wuni River, North and South Stone Pillars areas near Guyuan are under the jurisdiction of Fengning County, Jehol. The Chahar Provincial Government immediately negotiated with Matsui, the Japanese Liaison Officer stationed in Zhangjiakou. Ping Fang also filed a negotiation with the Japanese Embassy, and the military attache Takahashi telegraphed the Japanese army in Jehol and agreed to use diplomatic means to explain the misunderstanding, considering it a local incident to be resolved locally. Our side sent personnel from the Chahar Provincial Government to investigate, and Matsui from the Japanese side went to Chahar Eastern to investigate the truth. He returned to Zhangjiakou the day before yesterday. Yue Kaixian, the Diplomatic Commissioner of Chahar, returned to Zhangjiakou from Beiping yesterday, arriving at 6:00 PM in the evening, and started negotiations with the Japanese representative in conjunction with Qin Dechun. Yue Kaixian and Matsui are old classmates and have excellent relations, making negotiations easier. The Longliang, Wuni River, North and South Stone Pillars areas belong to Chahar territory, as evidenced by Chinese and foreign maps. The boundaries are clear. The area has always been defended by local militias, and there are no formally stationed Chinese troops, which is also a fact. It is difficult to fabricate something out of nothing and call a deer a horse. Since both parties filed negotiations, the situation in Chahar Eastern has slightly eased. The Longliang, Wuni River, and other places are still defended by local militias, and it has been peaceful in recent days. Zhangjiakou receives daily telegrams from Beiping, reporting on the situation at the front. The following is the gist of the telegrams from yesterday and today: (1) The Japanese puppet troops on the Jehol border are still stationed in the same place. The militias in Longliang, Wuni River, North and South Stone Pillars, etc., have not withdrawn, and order remains the same. The locality is peaceful. (2) Chahar Eastern has been peaceful in recent days. Our militias are still defending the Longliang, Wuni River, North and South Stone Pillars area. Although the Japanese attitude has eased after Matsui, the Japanese Liaison Officer stationed in Zhangjiakou, went to Chahar Eastern for inspection, the issue has not been completely resolved and negotiations with Matsui are continuing. It is said that the Japanese puppet troops discovered in Datang the day before yesterday have retreated. The situation in Chahar Eastern has indeed eased in recent days. Today, representatives from both sides began negotiations in Zhangjiakou. The person in charge on the Japanese side is Matsui, and the person in charge on our side is Qin Dechun and Yue Kaixian, etc. As the situation in Chahar Eastern has eased, Song Zheyuan, the Chairman of Chahar, will not return to Chahar during the Lunar New Year. Qin Dechun will come to Beiping once negotiations have made some headway. (January 22)

Zhejiang Province Telephone Progress 126

Installation of Long-Distance Repeater Machines

Establishment of Public Telephones for the Masses

Hangzhou Dispatch: Since Director Zhao Zengjue took office at the Provincial Telephone Bureau in the summer of the 21st year [of the Republic, i.e., 1932], he has been determined to rectify various facilities. As a result of two years of diligent promotion, a provincial telecommunications network has been completed. Recently, to promote the enterprise, repeaters have been installed for long-distance telephones to increase transmission efficiency. For local telephones, public telephone agencies have been established to promote widespread use. In addition, measures for news communication via telephone have been established to facilitate news reporters' use of telephones to transmit news. Details are as follows: (1) Installation of Repeaters: In order to improve the effectiveness of long-distance telephones and clearly transmit sound waves, the Provincial Telephone Bureau specially ordered repeaters from abroad and completed their installation in Hangzhou. Trial use began a few days ago. From Ningbo to Shanghai Jiangwan and the new urban area, the sound waves were exceptionally clear and the results were excellent after testing using the repeaters. The bureau is also testing long-distance telephones in the remote counties of Wenzhou and Chuzhou in order to communicate directly with Shanghai, so that communication over hundreds of miles is no different from communication within the city. (2) Establishment of Public Telephones for the Masses: To facilitate the use of telephones by the people of Hangzhou, the Provincial Telephone Bureau is establishing public telephone agencies in Hangzhou. Reputable stores and alleys along the lines can apply to operate them. The payment methods are divided into two types: ordinary and special. Ordinary ones are exempt from installation fees, and each call is calculated at two cents and eight mills. Special ones are charged according to the city telephone regulations, and the monthly rent is charged according to Type C users, which will be implemented immediately. (3) Jiang-Zhejiang News Telephone Communication to be Implemented Next Month: In order to enable news reporters to transmit news via telephone, the Provincial Telephone Bureau has drafted preferential measures similar to the news telegraph regulations and sought the consent of the Jiangsu Provincial Government. With the agreement of both parties, the two provinces of Jiang-Zhejiang can communicate news by telephone, which is scheduled to be implemented on February 1. News reporters in Nanjing and Suzhou can make calls with news telephone certificates. The Zhejiang Telephone Bureau has already started issuing these certificates through the Business Section within days. (23rd)

Songjiang

Dredging of the South Salt Iron Ditch to Commence Soon 127

The South Salt Iron Ditch in Punan, more than thirty li long, is the hub for reaching various towns in Punan. It has not been dredged for nearly forty years, resulting in siltation and impassable waterways. Yesterday, County Magistrate Jin led Section Chief Xu Mojia of the Technical Section to the Tingyu Huan'an Town to meet with local gentry Yang Chengfu to discuss dredging measures. A decision was made to proceed with the work, and the dredging personnel will commence work in mid-February. A special request for funding has been submitted to the Construction Department. In addition, the Changshan River dredging project has also been scheduled to commence simultaneously with the city river in mid-February to promote water conservancy.

Entire Jinshan Party Committee Resigns 128

The executive and supervisory committee members of the Jinshan County Party Headquarters, Lü Xiao, Xiao Yongjiang, Ye Jiarui, Wang Qiyuan, and the alternate executive and supervisory committee members, jointly submitted their resignation to the Provincial Party Headquarters, stating in brief that they were elected as executive and supervisory committee members by the Delegates' Congress in the 22nd year [of the Republic, i.e., 1933] and approved by the committee for record. Since taking office, it has been more than a year. Reflecting on themselves, they feel inadequate in learning and lack experience. Moreover, the county party's funds are insufficient each month, and personnel and administration are handled in accordance with the regulations. There is no way to make up for the deficits. Furthermore, local politics are not well-managed, construction is not thriving, and corruption is rampant. Repeated reports have been made, but to no avail. They feel it is difficult to handle affairs in this environment, so they specifically submit their resignation, hoping for approval.

Suzhou

Joint Defense Meeting of Two Counties 129

The water and land police teams of Wujiang and Wuxian counties, in order to maintain the security of the four rural areas during the winter defense period, plan to implement joint defense. They held a joint defense meeting of the two counties at the Wujiang County Public Security Bureau yesterday (23rd). The chairman, Nie Dezhao (attached to the Wuxian Security Brigade), decided on the spot that each of Wujiang and Wuxian counties should send a security team to be stationed in the Yinshan Jiapu Bridge area at the border of the two counties. In case of bandit alerts, they will be dispatched at any time to maintain land defense. As for water defense, it will be the responsibility of the various sub-teams of the Water Public Security Second District to patrol for a long period of time, and joint sentry duty will be implemented from today to facilitate communication.

Wuxi

Lawyer Arrested by Head of Criminal Prosecution Bureau 130

Sun Wenying, a local resident, also known as lawyer Sun Zuhong, is the younger brother of former County Magistrate Sun Zuji. The other night, Sun and his friends Zhu Yunsheng and others were chatting in Room 59 of the New World Hotel and playing donkey cards. Inspector Feng of the Public Security Bureau discovered them and took them to the bureau. Section Chief Yi Weifan opened the court. Sun and others argued that donkey cards are popular in Europe and the West and are the same as chess in China, so they did not admit to gambling. However, Section Chief Yi still sentenced them to a fine of ten yuan for similar gambling. Sun and others immediately requested to read the statement and found that the statement recorded that Sun and others had admitted to gambling, so they requested a correction, but it was not allowed. Then they declared that they did not accept the punishment and requested that the fine be changed to a deposit, retaining the right to appeal, which was also not allowed. Afterwards, Sun and Zhu published advertisements in the local newspaper, declaring the illegal actions of the Public Security Bureau. On the one hand, they sued Chen Yuchu, the director of the Public Security Bureau, and Section Chief Yi Weifan in the local branch court for abusing their power and infringing on their freedom. On the other hand, Inspector Feng of the Public Security Bureau also sued Sun and others in court for defamation by publishing in the newspaper. At the same time, more than ten lawyers from this county, including Zhou Jiapu, Zhou Beiwu, and Li Yaochun, said that the people did not accept the Public Security Bureau's punishment for violating the law and could file an appeal according to the law. The Supreme Court had issued Interpretation No. 701 in the 21st year [of the Republic, i.e., 1932]. The bureau took advantage of its power to play with the law, depriving the people of their rights, and changing the statement. All the truth and falsehood should be thoroughly investigated. Yesterday, they specifically sent a joint telegram to County Magistrate Yan, requesting a fair and thorough investigation.

County Government Burns Exhibits in Drug Case 131

The county government of this county has been handling cases of drug use since June to September last year, totaling 49 cases. All the exhibits confiscated in each case, amounting to more than a thousand pieces, were burned in the open space of the county government yesterday morning at 10 o'clock. Bai Zhujun, a training officer from the Zhenjiang Garrison Headquarters, was dispatched to supervise nearby, and representatives from various agencies and groups also went to observe. County Magistrate Yan ordered the police to take the drugs out of the warehouse, place them on firewood, pour kerosene on them, and set them on fire. It took an hour to complete.

Changzhou

Monk in Temple Murdered by Bandits for Money 132

Mingyi, the abbot of the Shemiao Temple in Maosi Turen Lane, Cheng Yizhen, Wu County, is 60 years old. Because the temple has no property and there are no other monks or incense followers, only Mingyi lives in the temple, chanting scriptures and selling services for a living. He is diligent and thrifty, and has saved a little money in the past ten years. However, bandits learned of this and went to kill him on the night of the 20th of this month. All the money and miscellaneous items were robbed. After Mingyi was killed, no one outside knew about it. It was not until the evening of the 22nd, when a water chestnut seller went to ask for money, entered the temple and shouted for the old monk, but there was no sound. Then the corpse was found in the stove, which was very shocking. He ran to tell the neighbors, and they went to check together. They saw that the monk's head had multiple knife wounds, and there were blood stains everywhere in the temple. All the miscellaneous items were messed up. It was undoubtedly a murder for money. The Public Security First Branch dispatched police to the temple to investigate and reported to the County Court Prosecutor's Office to send personnel to inspect on the 23rd in order to arrest the murderer and investigate the case.

Soviet Embassy's Statement on the Illegal Sale of the East Road Issue 136

The Soviet Union Recognizes the "Puppet State" as the Local Government of the Three Northeastern Provinces

That Local Authority Has Precedents for Negotiating with the Soviet Union on the East Road

The Shanghai Office of the China Eastern Railway Has Nothing to Do, So It Is Being Abolished

China United News Agency reports from Shanghai that, according to a Japanese telegram yesterday, a compromise has been reached in the illegal negotiations between Japan and the Soviet Union, and a formal signing is scheduled for next month. A reporter from China United News Agency visited the Shanghai office of the Soviet Embassy at 11 a.m. yesterday. The acting ambassador, Mr. Spifanyarak, and Secretary Mirivaneski received them. According to them, the Shanghai office of the Soviet Embassy has not received a formal report from the Moscow government. Whether the news of the success of the East Road negotiations is true cannot be confirmed. Before receiving formal information, it is not convenient to express an opinion. When asked whether this would violate the Sino-Soviet Agreement of 1924 regarding the East Road, Mr. Mirivaneski replied that, in his personal opinion, the Chinese government cannot exercise management rights over the East Road. Although the Soviet Union does not recognize "Manchukuo," it recognizes the Manchurian authorities as the local government of the Three Northeastern Provinces as before. The local government of the Three Northeastern Provinces has precedents for conducting diplomatic negotiations with the Soviet Union to resolve the management of the East Road. When asked whether the abolition of the Shanghai office of the China Eastern Railway was related to the Soviet Union's abandonment of the East Road, he said that the office had nothing to do in Shanghai and was useless, so it was abolished.

Second Strike at Twelve Forts Blocks Haizhou Salt Transport 140

Huai salt is usually loaded onto ships at Jiangzikou, Haizhou, and other places to Twelve Forts, and then loaded onto steamships to be transported to various ports along the Yangtze River. Since the last strike occurred, the salt affairs authorities have complied with the requests of the salt transport workers and junk boatmen to allow half of the ships to remain in Twelve Forts for transshipment. Unexpectedly, after the strike was resolved, the salt workers in Twelve Forts claimed that they could not get half of the work, and a second strike broke out suddenly. Not only Twelve Forts, but even Pukou was affected.

Workers Detain Merchant Ships 141

When the strike occurred, the salt workers tried their best to sabotage the salt loading work in order to achieve their goal of stopping the strike. The various merchant ships in Shanghai that had already signed contracts to transport Huai salt to Chu initially did not know about this. Some of them sailed to Haizhou to load salt. For example, a certain merchant ship in Shanghai arrived in Haizhou the day before yesterday. Before it could be loaded, it was discovered by the strikers, who immediately detained the ship and sent people to guard it, not allowing it to be loaded. They even threatened that if any more merchant ships tried to load salt and disrupt their strike, they would dismantle the ships.

Salt Transport Completely Stalled 142

After the Yuanxing ship unloaded the timber at Dapu, it was originally scheduled to load salt to transport to Han. Unexpectedly, the strike broke out suddenly, and some salt transport ships had already been detained. The ship was deeply afraid of accidents, so it immediately stopped transporting salt and returned to Shanghai empty. The various ships in Shanghai that had already signed leases to transport salt to Han, after hearing this alarming news, were also afraid of unexpected damage and stopped loading one after another. Salt transport has been blocked.

Settlement of Cross-Border Road Construction and Electricity Rights 143

Talk by Xu Peihuang of the Municipal Public Works Bureau

Shanghai Times News Agency reports that the electricity issue regarding cross-border road construction in this city has been formally signed this month, after the long term negotiation between both sides. The Shanghai West Electricity Co., Ltd. has been announced to be established in name. Yesterday, Xu Peihuang, director of the Public Works Bureau, issued a statement regarding the progress of the situation. According to Xu, due to various circumstances, the time taken in the middle was quite long for the electricity issue regarding the cross border roads. However, as of recently, all settlements have been reached and the agreement has been formally signed on the fourth of this month. The agreement was jointly signed by the mayor and the general manager of the electricity company. The contents of the agreement consist of the electricity company paying a one-time franchise fee of 1.5 million yuan. The operating period is set at 30 years. Upon the expiry of the period, the municipal government has the priority right to receive an appraisal. In addition, during the monopoly period, the company will pay 5% of its operating income to the municipal government annually as remuneration. According to the above agreement, in order to handle the power supply matters in the western district of Shanghai, the Shanghai West Electricity Co., Ltd. will be established. The company is required to have a capital of 6 million yuan, of which the electricity company accounts for 51% and Chinese business accounts for 49%. The business scope mainly includes electric lights, electric power, and electricity industry. Currently, the franchise fee of 1.5 million yuan has been paid to the municipal government by the electricity company in one lump sum. As for the Shanghai West Electricity Co., Ltd., it has been announced in name since the establishment of the agreement. However, in fact, various registration procedures are currently being submitted to the municipal government and the Public Works Bureau for processing. It is also heard that all 6 million yuan of stock have been raised and can be formally established within the next one or two months. As for the recent dissenting remarks from the side of the board of works, this is the electric power supply right of the public concession of the Shanghai Electricity Co., Ltd., which was paid by the board of works, or there may be some points of discussion in their mutual agreement, but generally speaking, there should be no problem for the Shanghai West Electricity Co., Ltd.

Banking Sector Low-Interest Loans to Support Industry 144

Cannot Be Achieved Without Government Subsidies

And Interest Rates on Depositors Must Be Reduced

丨A Conversation with a Certain Banker丨

Guowen News Agency reports that the cotton industry in our country has recently suffered from the impact of expensive cotton and cheap yarn, as well as the dumping of inferior goods, which has resulted in the closure of many spinning mills. It was reported a few days ago that Nie Lusheng, a leader in the cotton industry, said that the reason for the failure of the cotton industry was due to high interest rates, and suggested that various banks organize a cotton industry banking group, and the interest on loans to cotton mills should not exceed 4%. The loss beyond that should be compensated by government allocations. According to a certain banker interviewed by reporters yesterday, the rescue of Chinese factories by the banking sector is an obligation that should be fulfilled. The plan to reduce loan interest rates was proposed several years ago, but it ultimately failed because the national treasury was in deficit and could no longer allocate funds to compensate for this loss, so it was disbanded. Now that someone has raised this issue again, if the government can deposit funds with an interest rate of 70 to 80 mills, or even 1%, the loans that are released will inevitably be above 70 to 80 mills. Therefore, the banking sector alone cannot think of a way. If foreign banks are used as a comparison, the interest rate on deposits in foreign banks is only 1% to 2%, so the interest rate on loans only needs to be 3%.

Currently, after discussion by the subscribers, it is believed that unless the non-performing portion is collected and supplemented, it may affect the overall business in the future. It is therefore necessary to temporarily delay the payment. Our company has had both the fact of closing down and the fact of opening the door to make payments for two days, and we are unwilling to lose all our efforts. We must strive to remedy the complete integrity in the shortest possible time and continue to make payments. Wing On Silver Company, January 23.

Reduction of Foreign Troops Stationed in Shanghai 150

But the Total Number of Japanese Troops Remains the Same

The Shanghai Times reports that the number of foreign troops stationed in Shanghai has decreased significantly in the past two months. The Vietnamese troops returned to Vietnam, and the French troops returned to France. As for the total number of British troops stationed in Shanghai, it has not decreased compared to two months ago, but at the beginning of last year there were two battalions, and now there is only one battalion left. Only the Japanese troops have not decreased. Although the troops stationed in Shanghai have changed several times, the total number remains the same as before.

Representatives from Five Exchanges Rushed to Beijing Last Night 152

Each Carrying a Letter of Opinion to Vigorously Argue before the Assembly

The Cotton Cloth Brokers Association Submits a Request for Delay

The Shiye News Agency reports that since the Ministry of Finance announced the scheduled imposition of a transaction tax, the five exchanges in this city immediately held joint meetings to appeal to the Central Political Council, the National Government, Chairman Chiang, and various ministries and departments, requesting exemption. The Ministry of Finance submitted the matter to the Finance and Economics Committees of the Legislative Yuan, which will review it again today. Because the exchanges received a notice from the Legislative Yuan, they specially dispatched eighteen representatives last night at eleven o'clock, carrying letters of opinion from each exchange, to rush to Beijing on the Beijing-Shanghai express train to participate in the meeting, consult on everything, and pre-determined three measures in a joint meeting to submit to the assembly for discussion. The details are as follows:

Joint Meeting Proposes Three Measures 153

Yesterday, the five exchanges of this city—cotton cloth, gold, securities, flour, and miscellaneous grains—in addition to having the chairmen of each exchange prepare a reply to the notice from the Legislative Yuan and a petition, convened a joint meeting to discuss three measures to request from the Legislative Yuan: (1) request the withdrawal of the proposal to levy taxes; (2) temporarily postpone the levy (if the above two items cannot be done, then the following third measure will be used to request a reduction in the tax rate, and it must be achieved); (3) reduce the percentage, predetermining 0.0025% for marketable securities, that is, a tax of 2.5 cents for every 10,000 yuan of transaction (the Ministry of Finance has revised this to 0.0125%); cotton, cotton yarn, flour, and miscellaneous grains are all reduced to 0.0005%, that is, a transaction tax of 5 cents is levied for every 10,000 yuan (the Ministry of Finance has set the tax at 72.5 cents per 100 piculs of cotton, 3.075 yuan per 100 bales of cotton yarn, 57.5 cents per 1,000 bags of flour, and 1.275 yuan per 1,000 catties of miscellaneous grains). The brokers associations of the other exchanges also held meetings yesterday afternoon to discuss ways to vigorously argue for their case, prepare letters of opinion outlining the difficult circumstances of each exchange, and at eleven o'clock yesterday afternoon, they accompanied the chairmen of each exchange, carrying important documents, to Beijing. The list of representatives includes Cotton Cloth Chairman Mu Ouchu, Brokers Association Bian Futang, Wu Xunqing, Shao Wenmei; Miscellaneous Grains Chairman Gu Xinyi, Brokers Association Xue Chengzhang, Xu Jianqi; Securities Chairman Zhang Weiru, Brokers Association Wang Zhengru, Wu Limen, He Peiyuan; Flour Chairman Wang Yiting (due to illness, entrusted to Gu Xinyi to represent); Brokers Association Zhang Weiyun, Wang Zhongliang, Yang Jingcheng; Gold Chairman Xu Busun, Brokers Association Zhan Liansheng, Ren Jiafu, and seventeen others.

Cotton Cloth Brokers Association Petition 154

Yesterday, the Shanghai Chinese Cotton Cloth Exchange Brokers Association submitted a document to the Finance and Economics Committees of the Legislative Yuan, stating: "In order to deliberate on the transaction tax and explain the difficulties of business, this association previously submitted details of the commercial difficulties and inability to bear the burden to the Ministry of Finance on several occasions. Now we have received a notice from your committee stating that the case is about to be reviewed and requesting us to send representatives to state our opinions, showing the utmost intention of your committee to consult widely and be open-minded. Now, this association dares to present the true difficulties of business, which were not covered in the previous submission, and humbly ask for your consideration. Recently, due to the bankruptcy of rural villages in the interior, the purchase of cotton has decreased, resulting in various groups stationed in Shanghai and yarn merchants closing down due to the lack of business. Yarn factories and cotton merchants in various places are also reducing their activities on the exchange due to financial constraints and lack of turnover. On the other hand, foreign firms, due to the recession in their own countries in recent years, have also broken various precedents (such as waiving margin money and reducing commissions), giving preferential treatment to customers and competing for Chinese business, resulting in the increasingly depressed state of the business of this association's merchants and their gradual decline. (Omission) Based on the above-mentioned reasons, the difficulties of this association's merchants are becoming increasingly apparent and need not be concealed. If a transaction tax is added, this burden will be difficult to pass on in today's extremely depressed industrial and commercial environment. The result will not only be the further decline of this association's merchants' business and its virtual stagnation, but also the further decline of the depressed commercial situation and the transformation of the stagnant economy into panic, which is contrary to the government's original intention of opening up financial resources and promoting industry and commerce. Therefore, we dare to make another appeal when your committee deliberates, humbly requesting your committee to understand the people's hardships, consider the overall situation, and approve the postponement of the case. We are eagerly awaiting your order. Respectfully submitted to the Finance and Economics Committee of the Legislative Yuan, representative of the Shanghai Chinese Cotton Cloth Exchange Brokers Association, Bian Futang."

Cotton Cloth Exchange Submits Document to the Ministry of Industry 157

Responding to the Hua Shang Yarn Factory's Request to Stop Auctioning Cotton

The Cotton Cloth Exchange submitted a document to the Ministry of Industry, responding to the Hua Shang Yarn Factory's claim to ban speculation, restrict trading, and stop auctioning cotton, stating: "We submit this petition. Recently, we saw in the newspaper that Wuxi Shenxin and other yarn factories, and Shanghai Wing On and other yarn factories, submitted documents to various ministries and departments of the central government, requesting the banning of speculation, restricting trading, and stopping the auctioning of cotton in order to maintain the textile industry. They made many accusations against our exchange, but completely ignored commercial facts and the law, even claiming that this association is like the East India Company, and only by destroying and eliminating it can the crisis of the yarn industry be saved and the decline of the country be rescued. The strangeness of this argument is truly shocking. Without clarification, the truth will be obscured, making it difficult for the factories to be convinced and confusing the public. Therefore, before responding to each item, we will first briefly summarize the system and functions of the exchange as an outline. The exchange is a product of modern economic organization. European and American countries initiated it first, Japan followed, and China followed Japan. The reason for needing this organization is that modern market trade is becoming increasingly complex and competition is fierce. Without the formation of a publicly determined market price, it is not enough to reflect the actual situation of supply and demand in the market. Without the opportunity for hedging, it is not enough to allow the business community to operate freely. Without a centralized location for large-scale buying and selling, it is not enough to allow both supply and demand to be coordinated. The exchange was created to meet this need and is a necessary stage in the process of modern economic organization. Only because of this, if there is no exchange, then so be it. If there is an exchange, it cannot allow its buying and selling to be limited to the same industry. The exchange is originally a mechanism for buying and selling between supply and demand. Since supply and demand are not exclusively for the same industry, the exchange's buying and selling cannot be limited to the same industry. If it is limited to the same industry, it is to control and monopolize the market price of the nation's supply and demand with a small number of businesses in the same industry, leading to many malpractices. China's Exchange Law and the exchange laws of other countries have not set this restriction, probably because they know that setting this restriction is absolutely impossible in reality and would completely eliminate its ability to stabilize prices and regulate supply and demand. Furthermore, the buying and selling of the exchange cannot be called empty selling. Empty selling refers to not providing goods for delivery or not providing funds for delivery at the time of delivery. If the buying and selling of the exchange is based on providing goods or funds for delivery as a principle, before the delivery date, both the buyer and seller may resell and buy back to settle, but once the delivery period arrives, the buyer must prepare sufficient funds to receive the goods from the seller, and the seller must prepare sufficient goods to demand payment from the buyer. If one party cannot fulfill its obligations, it should be subject to penalties for breach of contract. This is the general rule of any exchange transaction. Therefore, when buying and selling in the market, no matter how large the amount bought or sold is, since it cannot be predicted that there will be no goods to provide for delivery at the time of delivery, it cannot be called empty selling. If it is said that empty selling refers to having no actual goods in hand when buying and selling, then when manufacturers sell forward yarn on the exchange, the yarn has not yet been spun, so how can there be so-called actual goods? It is only that the manufacturer sells forward yarn to the customer, giving only a piece of order. The customer can then sell it on the exchange. When the order expires, the manufacturer often only delivers a few percent due to insufficient allocation of goods and cannot deliver the full amount. The customer has no choice but to buy back the missing amount on the exchange to avoid being penalized for breach of contract. This often happens. In this situation, not only does the customer have no actual goods in hand when selling in the market, but the manufacturer also has no so-called actual goods when selling to the customer. Therefore, empty selling refers to buying and selling where the obligation to deliver cannot be fulfilled at the time of delivery and can never be said to be empty selling simply because there are no actual goods in hand when buying and selling on the exchange. Once this meaning is clear, the factories' request to ban empty selling on the association is aimless and not worth refuting. However, for the sake of clarity, we must explain each of the items listed in the original petition. According to the original petition, "The purpose of the exchange is to regulate supply and demand and stabilize prices. However, the brokers do not limit themselves to acting as agents for buying and selling for businesses in the same industry. Anyone only needs to pay a small amount of margin money to speculate, or even rely entirely on credit, and the margin money is also waived. Therefore, tens of thousands of bales of cotton yarn and hundreds of thousands of piculs of cotton are traded every day, but the number of deliveries at the end of the month is always less than one percent, which is pure speculation." The mission of the exchange is to regulate supply and demand and stabilize prices, but everyone must have the opportunity to entrust brokers to buy and sell in order to regulate, and both supply and demand must adopt a competitive buying and selling method to exchange what is available for what is not, and to help each other in order to stabilize. If it is said that only those in the same industry can buy and sell on the exchange, then all suppliers and demanders must be in the same industry. If not, how can the exchange complete its mission of regulating and averaging? Furthermore, China's Exchange Law only has the name of the client and does not stipulate that the client's qualifications are limited to businesses in the same industry, which clearly shows that the so-called client refers to the general public. However, the original petition actually used the fact that the brokers' buying and selling on behalf of customers is not limited to businesses in the same industry as a reason, and we truly do not know what it is based on. Furthermore, regardless of the amount of the brokers' buying and selling, they must pay margin money to the exchange in accordance with regulations. If the exchange believes that there is a large amount of buying and selling or that the market price is at risk of sharp increases or decreases, it can collect special margin money from them at any time to show restriction. It can be said that the exchange's supervision of brokers is extremely strict and its prevention is extremely close. As for brokers' collection of margin money from customers, they usually also collect margin money in accordance with regulations. Although there are occasional cases where a portion is collected or the entire amount is waived based on credit, it is purely a relationship of trust between the broker and the client. The exchange recognizes the broker as the main body of the transaction and should not interfere too much in this kind of behavior. How can this be blamed on the exchange? As for the amount of actual deliveries at the end of each month being less than one percent, this is an inevitable phenomenon of the exchange. Since the exchange has the fact of hedging and the method of reselling and buying back, buying and selling every day is extremely free. There is no need to wait for delivery day to deliver, and it can be settled at any time. Furthermore, in terms of delivery, there are two types: self-delivery and actual delivery. Actual delivery refers to the exchange executing the delivery on the delivery date. If the brokers contact each other properly before each delivery, deliver themselves, one party delivers the goods, and the other party receives the money to save procedures, it is called self-delivery. Therefore, it is not surprising that the amount of actual deliveries each month is less than one percent of the amount of buying and selling each month. Looking at the securities exchange, the amount of buying and selling each month reaches tens of millions, but how much is actually delivered? The amount of buying and selling on the gold exchange is also not less than thousands or tens of thousands each month, but the amount actually delivered is not only less than one percent, but even less than one-tenth of one percent. Furthermore, this is not only the case with exchanges in our country, but also with exchanges in other countries. However, the original petition actually pointed to this as evidence of pure speculation, not knowing what the word speculation means. If it is said that having no actual goods in hand when buying and selling in the market is speculation, then as we said before, there may not be actual goods in hand when buying and selling in the market, and manufacturers' hedging of futures cannot be uniquely different. Furthermore, Article 40 of the Exchange Law stipulates that "no one may establish a market similar to an exchange for the purpose of difference money trading outside the exchange for buying and selling," which clearly shows that difference money trading within the exchange is not prohibited by law. How can it be regarded as speculation and deeply hated? This is the first point. (To be continued)

Yarn Industry Association Submits Document to the Ministry of Industry 158

Requesting the Maintenance of the Yarn and Cotton Trading Market

The Yarn Industry Association submitted a document to the Ministry of Industry on January 22, stating: "We submit this petition, requesting the maintenance of the yarn and cotton trading market in order to facilitate sales and alleviate commercial difficulties. Recently, we saw in the newspaper that Chinese yarn factories are losing more than 20 yuan per bale of cotton yarn. Therefore, they jointly petitioned the government to send officials to Shanghai to conduct a thorough investigation of the actual situation and to order the Chinese Cotton Cloth Exchange to find ways to maintain a balance between the prices of yarn and cotton. If the manufacturing costs of 20s standard yarn (excluding unified taxes) converted from the standard cotton market scale of 430 catties are less than 45 yuan, the auction should be stopped. We are not in a position to comment on whether the manufacturing cost of 20s yarn per bale must be so high. However, in the past year, non-Chinese yarn factories have made substantial profits. The same industry, the same period, and the same location have such different profits and losses, which cannot be created by merchants manipulating and scheming for profit. At a time when rural villages are bankrupt and finances are exhausted, they actually want to indulge their own selfish desires, deceive the government, and ban the exchange in order to manipulate the market and achieve their goal of enjoying profits, so that we have no opportunity to hedge, which is truly shocking. There are many yarn factories in the country, in addition to Chinese factories, there are also many Japanese and British factories. We will not discuss how much their various expenses should be. However, we have been operating in cotton yarn with the responsibility of promoting domestic yarn. Since the September 18th Incident, no matter how much profit Japanese yarn has, we have ignored it. This spirit of sacrifice cannot be said to be weak. Furthermore, due to frequent banditry and repeated disasters in the country, the rural villages have been bankrupted, and purchasing power has been decreasing daily, causing our business to decline. Each month, various groups purchase cotton yarn, but before the goods are shipped, the domestic market price has already weakened, or they sell cotton yarn in the interior, but before they can make up for it, the market price has gradually increased. This is a commercial risk that cannot be avoided. Fortunately, there is the market of the Chinese Cotton Yarn Exchange, which allows them to hedge their sales or purchases, so that they can protect their losses in case of an emergency. Otherwise, our industry would have been wiped out long ago. Recently, we saw in a document from the Ministry of Finance to the Executive Yuan that merchants manipulate and scheme for profit, and that supply and demand rely heavily on the organization of the exchange as a medium. These are reasonable and famous words and should not be criticized. Furthermore, each factory is aiming for a cost of 45 yuan and is petitioning the government to order the exchange to comply. In addition to the exchange market price, each factory will also use this as the basis for its transactions with us. Otherwise, they will eat their own words and will not know how to face the government or the exchange. It is a strategy of driving fish into the abyss, which we do not approve of for yarn factories. Furthermore, since our industry is closely related to yarn factories, we sincerely hope that each factory can obtain a substantial profit of more than 20 yuan per bale in the natural trend. We dare to ask each yarn factory to work hard on mechanical improvement, production increase, cost reduction, and reasonable management to seek progress and not to hinder the business of others with strategies that abandon the fundamentals and pursue the superficial. Because the stakes are high, we earnestly request your ministry to uphold justice in order to prevent the abuse of monopoly. We are eagerly awaiting your order. Respectfully submitted to the Ministry of Industry, presenter, Shanghai Yarn Industry Association."

Shu Chushi Returned to Shanghai Only Yesterday Morning

The Cultural Relics to be Transported to England Will Be Selected Soon

The Xin Sheng News Agency reports that since the cultural relics stored in Shanghai from the Former Palace Museum were inspected by the cultural relic inspection specialist Shu Chushi, who was appointed by the Ministry of Education under the order of the Executive Yuan, and his assistant Xue Tiechen, who came to Shanghai last December, the cultural relics of the Ancient Artifacts Hall have been inspected successively for two months, totaling more than 400 boxes. Shu had to return to Beijing every Sunday of every one or two weeks to report to the Central Cultural Relic Preservation Committee. He still went to Beijing last Saturday (the 19th) as usual, because he attended the regular meeting of the Ancient Relic Management Committee and stayed in Beijing for several days. He returned to Shanghai only yesterday morning. The inspection of cultural relics continued yesterday morning. Shu Chushi, Ouyang Banghua, Xue Tiechen, and others went to the first warehouse on Tianzhutang Street before eight o'clock to work as usual. As for the cultural relics to be transported to England for the Ancient Relic Exhibition, it is heard that the Executive Yuan will send personnel to Shanghai to check the cultural relics in the current Qing Dynasty of the Ancient Relic Hall and the cultural relics of the Chenlie Institute that were selected. Last autumn, Lu Xirong, Fu Yiwen, and others were sent by the internal department to Shanghai to check the registration and sun-dry them. All were well preserved. Petition to the Seamen's Party Headquarters by the Bereaved Families of the Tongfu Steamer Incident 165

Solving the Compensation Problem

The Tongfu Steamer encountered a reef and completely sank in Korean waters. All fifty-six crew members perished. After the news was confirmed, various seamen's organizations in this port immediately petitioned the Special Seamen's Party Headquarters of the Republic of China and the Shanghai Municipal Social Bureau to form the Tongfu Steamer Seamen's Bereaved Family Relief Committee to handle compensation negotiations. The Special Seamen's Party Headquarters dispatched Mei Kaiyi and Wang Zhonggang to negotiate several times. Zhuo Huimin initially acted as the representative of Bao Anfu, the manager of the steamer company (Tong'an Company), to handle the case. Later, Bao also requested Shen Baolian and others to mediate. While the mediation was still in progress, Bao again entrusted lawyer Zhang Henghai to publish a notice in the newspaper, setting the amount of compensation and inviting the families to claim it. The families felt that the unilaterally determined amount was unfair and did not conform to Article 67 of the Maritime Law. Moreover, it was vastly different from the methods used for the China Merchants Bureau's Tunan Steamer and the Sanbei Company's Taishan Steamer. They again petitioned the Special Seamen's Party Headquarters, which dispatched Wang Zhonggang to negotiate directly with Zhang Henghai. Zhang indicated that he would consider it further. However, two days later, Bao Anfu again published an announcement in the newspaper (see the front page of the Shen Xin News on the 21st), distorting the Maritime Law and attempting to force the families to accept his unilaterally determined compensation. The families believed that the seamen were performing their duties while working and navigating on the ship. The ship's inadequate equipment and repeated accidents were sufficient proof of negligence. Recently, in Korean waters, the ship sank entirely, partly due to overloading with timber and partly due to hitting a reef. This was purely due to human error and should not be considered a natural disaster. The ship was insured in Japan, and Bao had already received the insurance money. Due to debt relations, he designated 40,000 yuan of the insurance money as compensation. Economically, Bao suffered no loss because of the insurance. However, the deaths of fifty-six people on board were a truly tragic and terrible disaster. Bao disregarded human feelings and national laws, and all the families resented and hated him. Bao himself returned to Shanghai from Japan and went into hiding, undoubtedly with others taking advantage of his absence to manipulate and monopolize everything, causing widespread anxiety. Yesterday, more than seventy family members gathered at the Chinese Jun'an Sailors' Public Association to discuss the final solution and petitioned the Special Seamen's Party Headquarters, requesting three points. Secretary Chen Songping of the Party Headquarters received them. The family representatives, including Chen Shenshi, recounted the case's progress: (1) They demanded that Bao Anfu be warned to appear and handle the matter within a time limit. (2) They insisted on receiving compensation according to the same methods as the Sanbei Company's Taishan Steamer. (3) If Bao Anfu continued to evade and not appear, they requested the Party Headquarters to petition the central government for a strict public wanted notice. After hearing the families' requests, Secretary Chen agreed to accept them and report them to Committee Member Yang for review.

Lawyer Liu Bin Referred for Disciplinary Action; High Court Orders Suspension of Duties 168

Yesterday, the Lawyers Association Was Ordered to Comply

Lawyer Liu Bin was previously prosecuted by the French Concession police for fraud. After the Second Special Court concluded the trial, he was sentenced to imprisonment. The court notified the Lawyers Association to suspend Liu Bin from his duties. Subsequently, Liu appealed against the verdict, and after retrial, he was sentenced to a fine of 800 yuan. After the verdict, Liu believed that according to the Judicial Yuan's interpretation, he could still serve as a lawyer after being fined, so he sent a letter to the Lawyers Association requesting to restore his membership. After the executive and supervisory meeting of the Lawyers Association passed the resolution, he was allowed to restore his membership. Now it is learned that the Third Branch of the Jiangsu High Court believes that although Liu Bin was spared criminal punishment, his actions violated the Lawyers' Regulations and was referred for disciplinary action. During the disciplinary period, he should still be suspended from his duties. Yesterday, a special order was issued to the Lawyers Association to investigate, and the original text is as follows: For the matter of issuing an order, it is approved that the Lawyers' Disciplinary Committee of this court sent a letter stating that the committee accepted the case of lawyer Liu Bin being referred for disciplinary action. During the investigation, it was determined that it was necessary to suspend the lawyer's duties first. In accordance with the provisions of Article 16, Paragraph 1 of the Lawyers' Disciplinary Committee Rules, a deliberation committee was convened at 1:30 PM on the 17th of this month to vote. The lawyer being referred for disciplinary action, Liu Bin, should be suspended from his duties first. The record is on file. In addition to sending the resolution to the Chief Prosecutor of the Shanghai Second Special District Court for investigation and handling, a corresponding letter is sent to your president for investigation. With this approval, in addition to distribution, the association is hereby ordered to be informed. It is reported that after receiving the order, the Lawyers Association has already complied.
