Shen Bao National Products Weekly

Words of Contribution

Thinking About the Future of the National Products Industry 284

— Yu Kangsheng

The teacher taught us to read a biography of Edison. From this book, we learn lessons that can be applied to our national products industry in two ways:

First, those with capital should organize consortia to provide the necessary living and experimental expenses for people with inventive genius, enabling them to imitate existing foreign goods and, even further, invent goods that foreign countries do not have. In the process of Edison's invention of the light bulb, all expenses were provided by American consortia. Although more than a year passed without solving the intended objective, the consortia still trusted him. It should be known that only with such good consortia in America could a great inventor like Edison emerge. Inventors are also human beings; if their basic needs for food, clothing, shelter, and transportation cannot be met, how can they concentrate on developing their inventive genius? Moreover, most of our inventors are trapped by financial constraints! Therefore, this is the first thing that should be done.

Second, the number of imitated products is increasing day by day, which is certainly progress in the national products industry; however, the fact tells us that many national products are made entirely of foreign raw materials, which is still somewhat unsatisfactory. When Edison invented the light bulb, the filament he used was obtained after testing 100,000 times on 6,000 kinds of bamboo filaments. The raw material for that bamboo filament came from Japan. Later, after many years of experimentation, he selected materials manufactured domestically to make the filament, abandoning Japanese goods. This is precisely the same work that we must do in the national products industry; otherwise, the more national products made entirely from foreign raw materials increase, the more the trade deficit will never decrease, because even if the people of the whole country buy national products, the national products manufacturers are directly importing foreign goods, so aren't the Chinese people indirectly selling foreign goods? Therefore, technical personnel of national products should try their best to research and discover them, and must not continue to be negligent.

I firmly believe that the realization of these two things is when the national products industry is on the right track. It will certainly lead to more significant progress than setting a National Products Year every year.

Students' Views on National Products in Various Countries 285

— Qin Jian

The calendar has turned to the first page of the twenty-fourth year, and it is said to be the third National Products Year. Although the import volume of cosmetics during the previous Women's National Products Year was somewhat uncomfortable, we can only say a silly self-deprecating remark, "The past is gone, the future can be pursued," under helpless circumstances—or what else can we do?

The third National Products Year has fallen on the students, who, as usual, have a relatively general level of knowledge, so the results this year may not be too unpleasant.

However, in a small number of cases, although a small number of students may attach a little more importance to foreign goods because they do not lack spending money and have more exposure to Western cultural relics, and they may regard foreign goods as noble and fashionable; however, it cannot be said that these students do not know how to love their country. At most, it is just that they (or she) do not have enough understanding of national products, and their views on the worship of foreign goods are wrong.

Therefore, while the curtain of this brand-new "Students' National Products Year" has just been raised, it may not be impossible to briefly mention the views of students in various countries on national products as a "mountain of assistance from others"?

(1) Japan 丨 To talk about students' views on national products, we must start with Japan. Before the Meiji Restoration, the domestic situation in Japan was as bad as the current situation in China: domestic production was scarce, and people had to obtain all daily necessities from foreign countries; and students (especially university students), because they had read a little Western books, everyone valued foreign goods very much. However, in the fifty or sixty years after the Meiji Restoration, on the one hand, the domestic productive forces have been strengthened, and the quality and quantity of all products have been greatly improved; and at the same time, the national authorities have also used various methods to encourage students to use national products 丨丨丨 For example, I heard that students at the Imperial University had to wear national product uniforms, and no matter how excellent their grades were, they would not be allowed to graduate. And in recent years, although nine out of ten students wear suits, 70-80% of the materials are their own domestic goods. The most surprising thing is the fountain pens they use—no matter how fashionable and noble the Parker and Conklin products from Europe and the United States are, they still honestly use their own "Taisho Mannenhitsu"!

(2) England——England is a country rich in conservatism and tradition, which everyone knows. Until now, the spirit of mercantilism is still quite preserved in their people. The country has always tried to increase exports; and the people, pay special attention to domestic goods. Students are especially so. From the time they are elementary school students, they have received traditional concepts in their families. As soon as they hear that something is "British," they immediately feel a sense of intimacy and glory. Growing up, it becomes an instinct. For daily necessities, from shirts to ties, from ink to tennis rackets, ice skates, cameras and other entertainment supplies, although German products are better than theirs, they still like to use "British" products. Even books and textbooks often have two versions, British and American. The binding and printing of the American version are more exquisite than the British version, but they choose the inferior domestic version to buy.

(3) France丨France is generally called "the country of fashion," The Country of Fashion, but their students' love for domestic goods is deeper than in other countries. The books, stationery, clothing, instruments, and cosmetics used by girls are either from Lyon or Paris. "French goods" are a supreme boast for French students.

(4) Germany丨Germany suffered a great loss in the European War, and the domestic situation was too bad; it was not easy for young people to go to school, and of course, it was impossible to purchase foreign goods. In these ten years of hard work, their students have completely developed a passion for using domestic goods.

The above is just a description of the situation in a few major countries. In the student circles of other countries, such as the United States, Russia, and Italy, they all have a special love for their own domestic goods. In this "Students' National Products Year," if Chinese students like to learn from foreign countries, then they can learn the virtue of their students' love for using national products.

Record of the Shanghai South National Products Exhibition 286

— Jia Guanjun

At 9 a.m. on January 6th, I was bored at home, so I went to visit the Shanghai South National Products Exhibition. It was a regular holiday on Sunday, so the number of visitors was even more crowded. Now, I will briefly record the highlights of the venue below:

The exhibition hall is located at the entrance of Hengxing Lane on Limatou Road in the 16th Puli of this city. There are two entrances and exits to the venue, both decorated with pine and cypress arches, with a national flag of the Kuomintang and another cloth banner with the words: "Shanghai South National Products Exhibition hosted by the China National Products Manufacturers Association welcomes visitors." There is also a couplet that says: "Promote Chinese National Products," "Work Hard to Save the Country with National Products."

There are more than a dozen factories displaying their products in the venue. The venue is a built-up shed, so it is high and bright. The exhibits are divided into categories such as cotton fabrics, silk fabrics, woolen fabrics, food, hardware, and leather. The best ones are the following three:

(1) The cosmetics of Shanghai Xiangpin Company, including powders, honey, rouge, perfume, essence, and Stancomb used by men and women. It is said that since the opening, female students from large, medium, and small schools in this city have purchased a lot, which shows a good phenomenon in the "Students' National Products Year."

(2) The glassware of the Central Chemical Glass Factory includes household teacups and vases, as well as glass tubes, glass pipes, glass covers, etc., totaling no less than twenty types, which shows a good phenomenon for the future of chemistry in our country.

(3) The educational supplies of Meilingdeng Factory include ink, colors, decolorizing water, advertising colors, economic ink, fountain pen ink, etc. It is said that the color of this ink does not change. The manufacturing method uses electric power to grind, so it is exceptionally fine. I bought a bottle of China Brand ink for only thirteen copper coins, which can be said to be cheap.

Several police officers stood in the venue to prevent petty theft. Outside the venue, there were outposts of the Shanghai South District East District Fire Brigade and the First Team of the Shanghai South District Security Corps to prevent accidents in the venue.

It is said that the exhibition period is only two weeks, but the daily business is over 15,000 yuan, which shows the general public's love for and use of national products. I visited the venue for a week, and there was no shortage of buyers, which shows the results of the public's improvement.

I hope that all students in large, medium, and small schools in the city will use national products during this "Students' National Products Year." First, it will not lose the value of the "Students' National Products Year," and second, it can develop our country's national products. All the talented students in the city should advocate and implement this.

▲The Student National Products Year Promotion Committee will convene its first executive board meeting in the coming days to discuss promotion methods and the establishment of branch associations.

It is heard that Mr. Zhang and others will begin to implement this plan upon their return to China, and many leaders in the city's business community have also expressed their support.

Interview Record

Nanyang Market Observation Notes (3) 287

— Ji Ping

A Conversation with Mr. Kang Yuan丨

(Question) Mr. Xiang, how do you think we should nurture roots and trunks?

(Answer) People in the country often believe that overseas Chinese in Nanyang are wealthy. I believe that people in the country may be even wealthier than overseas Chinese. However, the money of overseas Chinese circulates in the market. If they only have two or three coins, they will do the business of ten coins. Wealthy people in the country like to deposit money in banks, especially foreign banks. They have ten coins, but they are not willing to do the business of one coin. The same money, one dead and one alive, has a significant impact on the national economy and people's livelihood. In the country, I often hear a slogan: "Welcome overseas Chinese to invest in the motherland and develop industries." I think this is too biased. Overseas Chinese should invest in the motherland, and wealthy people in the country should also transfer capital to Nanyang to support the large and small industries and businesses operated by overseas Chinese. They deposit money in foreign banks, just wanting to rely on a British or American flag for protection. It is better to simply transfer capital to Nanyang and be sheltered by the entire foreign power. Isn't that more secure? This is not a joke. Many places in Nanyang really need Chinese to invest. Large and small industries are currently very depressed.

In my humble opinion, Nanyang lacks not only strong capital but also specialized talents. On the one hand, we need investment, and on the other hand, we also hope that excellent talents will go to develop. It is best for talents to follow capital. Once the capital goes, there will be a way for talents to go. In the past, people from Fujian and Guangdong could reach the other side for four or five yuan. Now it costs at least one hundred yuan. Moreover, the local government has set various harsh restrictions, and the landing procedures are very troublesome (especially in the Dutch East Indies). People in the country regard it as a daunting task. People who go abroad feel all kinds of suffering, and now it has become a situation of "those who want to go have no money, and those who have money don't go." It is best to use capital and talent together to seek common development. In short, those who are interested in Nanyang, whether they contribute money or effort, are directly related to the economy of overseas Chinese and indirectly related to the national economy and people's livelihood. This shows its importance. In the future, if overseas Chinese industries and businesses need capital, the country should find ways to provide assistance. If people without money want to develop in Nanyang, everyone should help them and organize immigration. This is exactly the principle of "making the best use of people's talents and making the best use of the land."

(Question) Which commodities are most needed in the Nanyang Islands at present?

(Answer) Cotton textiles, daily necessities, and silk are most widely needed. Although Western goods are available, their value is always higher than Japanese goods. People generally like to be greedy for cheapness, so Japanese goods naturally sell well everywhere. In terms of quality, Japanese goods only focus on form and are not durable. It is a pity that our domestic products are rarely found. Otherwise, comparing goods with goods, they are not inferior to Western goods.

Tender Skin 288

— Jing Tan

Many leaves in the corner of the wall gradually fade from withered green to burnt yellow, which symbolizes that the harsh winter is extending its power.

These days, Xiao Lan gets up early in the morning and goes to work. She walks on the road where the north wind is biting. She hides her hands in her pockets, but her tender skin is a little stinging from the cold wind. She is very annoyed! She is afraid that her skin will slowly freeze and crack, which is not very unsightly! She is not willing to learn from those rich ladies who spend a lot of money to buy imported beauty products. She thinks: "In this year of advocating domestic products for women, women are shamelessly buying foreign goods. Isn't that very shameful?" Therefore, although she has heard that "foreign honey" can protect the skin, she disdains to use it because it is a foreign product. She tried using domestic honey, but found it too sticky. This skin care problem really stumped her!

One day, Xiao Lan saw her girlfriend at her girlfriend's house pouring some white liquid from a flat glass bottle onto her face after washing her face.

"Why don't you have patriotism and want to use that kind of foreign honey?" Xiao Lan said with a reproachful tone.

"This is not foreign honey. This is domestic Xingqiu brand skin cream!" Her girlfriend said while handing over the flat bottle.

She took it in her hand and saw that there were indeed the words "Created by Wuzhou Pharmacy"; at the same time, she also learned that this domestic pure honey not only has good quality but also a lower price.

That day, Xiao Lan went to buy this domestic skin cream. From then on, she no longer feared the cold wind's invasion when walking on the road in the harsh winter.

Little Western Paradise 289

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter 8 A Remote Place with a Light Official, a Strong-Willed Order Arrives; a Grand Banquet in a Splendid Hall, Outside There is a Pitiable Worm

Just this sentence of his, outside the house, someone laughed loudly and said: I also agree! Good idea, good idea! That person also spoke with a Zhejiang accent and laughed as he entered. Zhang Jiefu thought, how could this person be so presumptuous? Looking at him, he was a man in his thirties, with a shaved head, a red face, and big eyes. He was wearing a blue wrinkled silk jacket and had rolled up his sleeves, revealing two thick arms, which gave him a bit of a sturdy appearance. Zhiqian smiled and offered him a seat and introduced him to both sides, saying that he was Magistrate Zhou. He laughed: What Magistrate Zhou, just Zhou Congda. Zhang Jiefu said: Your name is You Rong. He laughed: How does Mr. Zhang know? Jiefu said: I saw in the local newspaper that there is a Magistrate Zhou You Rong who has a good reputation for his administration, and he has asked for leave to come to Xi'an and is also staying at Little Western Paradise, so I guessed that. Zhou You Rong looked at Zhiqian and smiled slightly: I am worth something after all. People die leaving a name, and leopards die leaving their skin. I have earned a reputation for good administration. Haha! Actually, I don't have a good reputation for administration, I am disgracing myself, I was beaten up. I slept for two weeks after being beaten, and I couldn't do it anymore, so I took the opportunity to ask for leave and escaped to Xi'an. Zhang Jiefu was shocked when he heard this and asked: I forgot which county in the newspaper the Zhou Magistrate was in. Are the people in this county so fierce? Zhou You Rong laughed: If the common people beat me, what can I say? It must be that I am not doing my job well. Cheng Zhiqian laughed: Mr. Zhang, don't misunderstand. Three or four years ago, the county administration in the northwest counties was indeed difficult to handle. In the past two years, Shaanxi's politics has finally gotten on track. The counties in Guanzhong, in particular, are very orderly. It's just that on the extreme southern or northern borders, transportation is inconvenient. Official documents from Xi'an take two months to go back and forth. If there are old defense forces in that area and the finances are not circulating smoothly, there will be some constraints. Magistrate Zhou's county is located at the junction of three counties. The military leader there has been in office for the past five or six years, so he is not easy to deal with. (120)

Winter Weather Feels Like Spring 290

— Qing Qu

Isn't it already winter now? Hey! Then how does it feel like a mild spring? Could it be that the saying "If Heaven does not change, the Dao does not change" is really a bit wrong now? You! Don't you see the heavy fog covering us every morning? When we get up in the morning, it's not easy to see the person coming across from us. In the past, people said, "Three mornings of fog bring west wind," but unexpectedly, there is fog all the time, and the west wind refuses to blow. For a few days, it was like daytime darkness, with dense layers of clouds like they were about to press down, thinking that "Heaven was making snow up there," and soon it would snow heavily, turning into a silver world. Who knew that the morning light was clear, and a round of rising sun was shining in the eastern sky. The temperature not only did not drop but instead rose, it was as if spring had already arrived, and we were enjoying the warmth of the Qingming Festival. You think, isn't it strange!

What is most surprising is when you go to the suburbs and look around, the wheat in the fields is green and swaying in the wind, like green waves gently rippling. The wheat ears are just starting to sprout, and the broad beans are also developing especially well, with stems as tall as a foot, and the butterfly-shaped flower buds also seem to be flying, releasing a beautiful appearance. If you say it's not spring, where would you get this kind of scenery! Not only that, but sometimes you can also see the traces of flies and ants, they haven't disappeared yet. It's simply not winter, it's turned into spring. Some people say: This is God's kindness. Last year in the summer and autumn, it was hot and dry, and the common people suffered so much. They barely survived until today and haven't starved to death completely, and they can't withstand the great cold. So Heaven also had compassion and canceled this winter, advancing the spring weather ahead of schedule. I say that's right, but even if you have food and clothing, and you're burning a stove and wearing heavy furs, you must not be careless about health preservation.

Drops 291

— (Xiao Bai)

The comfort of travelers is hidden in the hands of those in green uniforms. The world's tombs can never bury human troubles.

People only know that marriage is the tomb of love, but they don't realize that graduation is the foundation of youth unemployment.

The world's disturbances and the darkness of society cause most people to feel a great deal of fear about the future, but I don't think so. The events of the future will always come, "Don't cry, don't laugh, deepen your understanding." We should embrace this attitude to welcome the future.

Seen on the Public Bus 292

— Mao Zhenyang

Today I went to Jing'an Temple for business. When I stepped onto the No. 7 public bus, I saw a handsome friend dressed in a Western suit and leather shoes sitting in the carriage. He arrogantly shifted his gaze to the outside of the window, resting his left leg on his right knee and constantly shaking it.

Before long, the bus started moving. After a while, it had already left Xujiahui and sped west. As usual, we all bought a ticket. Naturally, that Western-dressed friend was no exception. However, just as he was buying the ticket, a gust of wind blew, carrying the ticket he had bought out the window. He couldn't help but be stunned, but he still pretended to be indifferent and sat there. At this time, the ticket seller had already seen it and politely asked the Western-dressed friend to buy another ticket. However, not only did the Western-dressed friend refuse to buy another ticket, but he scolded the ticket seller. The ticket seller saw that he was very stubborn, so he softened.

Soon, a ticket inspector came along. He checked this friend and saw that he didn't have a ticket, so he asked him in a foreign language whether he had bought a ticket. But this friend had never studied foreign books, so he didn't understand at all and stood there dumbfounded in front of the foreigner, not even daring to take a breath.

At this time, the ticket seller had the upper hand and took the opportunity to show off his power, scolding the high-spirited Western-dressed young man until he didn't know whether to laugh or cry, even calling him a barber.

I sat next to him, watching the handsome friend with great surprise. Why didn't he even have the courage to speak in front of the foreigner! I was about to stand up and defend him, but he very quickly took out the money for another ticket from his pocket and paid it to the foreigner timidly. So I didn't say any more, only feeling that this Western-dressed friend had completely humiliated us Chinese people.

Fortunately, the terminal station arrived, and he quickly squeezed out of the crowd. When I got off the bus, he was already gone.

Records of Floating Fragrance of the Imperial Incense 293

— Originally Written by Princess Qing Deling, Translated by Qin Shouou

They bowed again and accepted the order. Standing side by side in front of the throne, they took out the almanacs and writing materials they had brought with them and began to calculate very solemnly. The Empress Dowager also sat upright and waited patiently for their reply. I happened to be standing behind the Empress Dowager at the time, witnessing them doing this futile and time-wasting thing. I couldn't help but laugh secretly, and I was also very anxious, fearing that they would calculate a bad result. Because I admired the scenery of Changbai Mountain and Songhua River even more than the Empress Dowager, and I had long wanted to visit, but I had no chance. This time I had arrived in Fengtian, and I happened to be with the Empress Dowager, so I was particularly excited to go, but I was afraid that these two old gentlemen from the Imperial Astronomical Bureau would make trouble for us! What particularly fascinated me was a passage recorded in a certain unofficial history, which described the birth history of our ancestors as absurd and beautiful as a myth. It said:

"Before the dates that can be checked in history, there was a small stream with clear water flowing in the wilderness near Changbai Mountain, and the fine and dense ripples were as beautiful as the scales on silver fish when illuminated by the sun. One early summer morning, the weather was particularly hot, and a girl from a family near the stream, known for her beauty, jumped into the stream to swim alone. As she was floating, she suddenly saw a bright red and lovely cherry floating on the green water. She found it interesting and quickly went over and picked it up and swallowed it in one bite. This was a very ordinary thing, and she didn't pay attention to it at all. Unexpectedly, after a few months, her belly gradually grew bigger, and people laughed at her for being pregnant without being married and discussed it. Only her parents knew that her behavior was usually very upright and didn't believe that she really had any shameful affair. But she was indeed pregnant, and eventually gave birth to a very fat boy. This boy was the ancestor of all Manchus...!" (230)

Begging Stick 294

— Wubian

I read in this newspaper the stories of the "Golden Carrying Pole" written by two gentlemen, which is indeed excellent after-dinner conversation material. Now the reporter will also write a good story about the "Begging Stick." Although it doesn't have much meaning, in these years when extravagance is prevalent, it may help the frugality movement and not violate the principle of showing frugality in national luxury.

This begging stick is still talked about in Huanan and Fengnan counties because the master of this story grew up in one of these two counties, although he has already passed away. What is the story? The master of the begging stick, because his family was destitute when he was young, and his parents both died, and he was young and had no ability to make a living, was forced by life to take a stick, carry a basket, and go out to beg. As the saying goes, "Begging for three years, lazy to be an official," not to mention that he had not received an education and had not learned a profession. Since he had embarked on this path of begging, he naturally made begging his proper profession. However, because he had endured hunger, cold, and hardship, he tried his best to economize in this begging process and did not spend half a cent lightly. In this way, little by little, he accumulated a lot of money after begging for decades. He used this money to buy land and cultivate it. Because of his frugal attitude in everything, he accumulated more and more, and almost became a well-to-do family. Then he built a house, married a wife, had children, and grandchildren. He transformed from a beggar into a wealthy elder. His family motto at that time was naturally no more than the four words "diligence and frugality." Moreover, he solemnly placed his begging stick in the main hall to show that he did not forget his roots and to use it as a warning for his descendants. Later, whenever his descendants disobeyed the family motto and wasted money for no reason, he would use this begging stick to warn and punish them. The descendants, thinking about the difficulty of starting a business, would repent.

After the master of the begging stick died, his grandsons gradually multiplied, forming a large clan. But they still kept the begging stick high, and whenever clansmen were unworthy, they would still use the begging stick to warn and punish them. So this begging stick still holds the highest authority in this clan.

Talking About the Philippine Carnival 295

— Yan Wenchun sent from the Philippine Islands

A few days ago, various Chinese newspapers announced that the Consul-General's Office had received a telegram from the Mayor of Shanghai, saying that Shanghai Chinese businessmen were enthusiastically preparing to participate in this year's Manila Carnival, and asked the Consul-General to help with everything, with the purpose of seeking Sino-Philippine friendship. The reporter asks to extract the nature and content of the conference so that our business community can have a little knowledge of what to follow.

The English word for Carnival is Carnival, which is the European and American Saint's Day Festival. After the Americans entered the Philippines, they began to hold it. It is purely a shareholder business, and the government is in a promoting and assisting position. There is a difference between old and new shareholders in each session. New shares pay a share of twenty yuan, which is given a beautiful badge, exempt from purchasing tickets, and can enter the auditorium for eight nights to watch various performances and dances. They have the right to vote for the Carnival Queen twice. Old shares pay only half the fee. In addition to being exempt from purchasing tickets, the rights enjoyed are also halved. As for the stock dividend, it disappears when the conference closes. Therefore, the income of the conference mainly comes from ticket stock payments, land rental fees (the area is divided and rented to private individuals for display or circus performances), and advertising fees (advertisements are painted on the surrounding walls).

The election of the Chinese Queen is also called Miss Philippines. In the initial election, newspaper readers have one vote per day for one month. Each registered newspaper can nominate a candidate, or they can freely print tickets for competitors to purchase more by paying a fee. Therefore, in the initial election, each newspaper can get more ticket sales. After the initial election is completed, the images of those elected are hung outside the office by the association for people to admire. A dance party is scheduled for the initial election winners and shareholders (non-shareholders can also purchase tickets to participate). Then the re-election begins. The right to re-elect is in the hands of the shareholders. Ladies from prominent families, wanting to inherit the vanity of this sixteen-night crown, instruct their relatives and friends to campaign for them. Sometimes the campaign is so intense that they cannot be elected without more than ten thousand shares. Therefore, begging for money is a common occurrence. Five years ago, the re-election system was changed, and a panel of judges was organized for aesthetic observation. All initial election winners had to wear swimwear and listen to male judges observing them closely. The Catholic Church strongly opposed this, and the number of shareholders suddenly decreased, so the old system was restored.

The structure of the venue is made of miscellaneous wood pillars, woven bamboo walls, painted in color, and installed with electric lights. Therefore, the lights are brilliant at night, and the layout of the ballroom is even more magnificent and gorgeous. The exhibits in the conference can be divided into three parts: (1) Public exhibits, that is, local products from various provinces and achievements from various agencies, such as schools and prisons, and forms from various departments and bureaus. (2) Merchant exhibits. (3) Various games, such as circuses, comedies, magic tricks, sleds, etc., all require the purchase of separate tickets. (4) Restaurants, pubs, and miscellaneous goods vendors. Four or five years ago, large quantities of domestic goods were transported from Tianjin, Shanghai, Fujian, and Guangdong for display. The National Government sent Vice Minister Mu Ouchu to the Philippines to participate in the grand event, and there was almost no day without welcome banquets. The heat of Sino-Philippine friendship naturally increased a bit as a result. Currently, the country is in great difficulty, and foreign aggression is urgent. Japan is eyeing East Asia, and the key players on the Philippine political stage all value the three islands of Japan. Japanese-Philippine friendship is sincerely hoped for, while Sino-Philippine friendship is a perfunctory formality. For example, this year's Far Eastern Games, which were supposed to be held in the Philippines, were succumbed to by Japan. The dissolution of the Far Eastern Games, which had a history of more than 20 years, is a rehash of old events and an international disgrace. From now on, we can only rely on national diplomacy to promote Sino-Philippine friendship, which may reduce the proposals in the parliament that treat overseas Chinese harshly. This is what our South Overseas Chinese sincerely pray for.

Participating in the exhibition can also find a way out for domestic goods, focusing on daily necessities. Cotton textiles from the Sanyou Industrial Society, canned goods from Shanghai Taifeng and Xiamen Taohua Datong, etc., are all suitable for Philippine consumption. If it is Fuzhou lacquerware, Jiangxi porcelain, antique bronze ware, and wood carvings, they are only for visitors to admire because they belong to decorations and have limited consumption. Among silk fabrics, scenery and figures that can be embedded in mirror frames are cheap and beautiful and also meet the need. In thatched cottages, almost every family hangs landscape paintings, so those seeking products should know what to pay attention to.

The conference is not only an entertainment institution for ordinary people, but because visitors gather in large numbers, the market can prosper. Moreover, if the political community wants to promote any cause, they can use this conference to promote it, which is easy to be effective. For example, eggs here originally came from China and Japan, with an annual leakage of more than 1.7 million pesos. The government wants to encourage the people to raise chickens, not only through written and pictorial propaganda but also by displaying chickens of various colors, and the hatching and feeding methods are arranged according to their progress. In addition, various chicken coops of different sizes are built, and courtyards in front of and behind houses can be developed into small-scale family chicken farms. The audience sees and hears, and in less than three years, chicken raising in various villages has become very effective. The import volume last year has been reduced by one-third.

Free Talk

Concerning the Question of the Interpenetration of Natural Science and Literature 296

— Meng Jia

Mr. Xiangshan, in his article "The Question of Mutual Interpenetration of Literature and Science,"

believes that the issue of interpenetration between natural science and literature is a matter of handling the subject matter, not a matter of method. Starting from this argument, Mr. Xiangshan proposes his "scientific literature that uses literary forms with natural science as the subject matter" and scientific fantasy novels. He regards this kind of scientific literature and scientific novels as the entire posture of the problem of the penetration of natural science and literature, and rejects the methodological problem of using natural science as an element of literary method.

I believe that Gao Erji's advocacy of "literary masters should assist practical scientific masters to express scientific thoughts, theories, and work in a simple and easy form" is only a tool for the popularization of science in the transitional period. As for whether this kind of scientific literature that uses literary forms to express natural scientific theories will still be necessary in the highest form of society in the future remains a question.

If we savor Mr. Xiangshan's opinions from another perspective, we find that they are inevitably narrow and mechanical. Because the issue of mutual interpenetration between literature and natural science is not only a matter of handling the subject matter but also a matter of method.

Mr. Xiangshan said: "As for those who advocate using natural scientific methods to deal with literature, description, and creation (?), analyzing psychology, heredity, etc., to achieve success, I disagree. If so, then Freud's psychological analysis should become the best method in literature, but the opposite is true. Our progressive method is based on social science."

This passage seems very thorough at first glance, but it is not so in practice. The statement that the progressive literary method is based on social science is only appropriate when it comes to the issue of a realistic and correct understanding. However, merely a realistic and correct understanding and the accumulation of common sense in social science cannot make literature. The main point is still the expression of images. My saying that the issue of mutual penetration between literature and natural science is a matter of method does not mean, as Mr. Xiangshan said, using natural scientific methods to deal with literature – if that were the case, then Mr. Xiangshan would certainly disagree. Mr. Xiangshan's opinion is somewhat based on the distortion or misunderstanding of this "methodological problem." My saying "also a matter of method" precisely means taking the subtle description of psychological or physiological changes, which have been further deepened and corrected due to natural science (psychology, physiology, biology, eugenics, genetics, etc.), as a comprehensive form, as an element of rich and colorful literary techniques. To attribute everything to physiology (sexuality...), psychology, heredity, etc., is the beginning of Freudianism and psychologism, which is certainly wrong.

Relying solely on the analysis of social scientific theories to obtain abstract concepts of social groups, characters, etc., cannot, in an artistic sense, become typical characters with distinct personalities. In China, as in Japan, the subjective depiction of conceptual ideas that simply expresses the analytical results of social scientific theories in literary form is the main shortcoming of early works of new literature. What we want to depict are living characters as cells of the real society. The lives of these living characters contain living joy, anger, sorrow, happiness, humor, love, hate, and other emotions, which intertwine and penetrate each other to form various typical personalities. Therefore, in a comprehensive form, the subtle description of the personality and psychological characteristics of various different characters is essential; without it, typification is impossible. Here, both social science and natural science play a role in the understanding of the class characteristics of the characters. We can never deny the influence of physiology and psychology on naturalistic writers such as Zola, nor can we deny the influence of medicine on the works of realist impressionist writer Chekhov. This influence can be clearly seen in the depiction of the pathological characteristics of characters, in the psychological description of the madman Ivan in "Ward No. 6," and in the description of the protagonist's neurosis in "The Black Monk."

However, what we cannot ignore in this regard is that the role of psychology in the realistic understanding and description of characters' psychology is only as a kind of guidance, just like social science in realistic understanding. As for the fact that the description of characters' personalities, psychology, consciousness, etc., cannot be separated from social conditions, it goes without saying.

Wu Family Restaurant 297

— Chen Fuxi

In Xuzhen, as long as you mention Wu Family Restaurant, everyone knows it: this is an old restaurant that opened before the Taiping Rebellion at the foot of Wolong Bridge.

"Wu Family Restaurant"

This large cloth signboard can be seen when you run down Wolong Bridge. Two wide frontages, with a second floor, very spacious. This old shop has maintained its reputation from before the Taiping Rebellion to the present, and no other restaurant has been able to compete with it. Because of this old signboard, there has never been a year of loss in the year-end settlement. In these years when all kinds of shops are opening, the business of Wu Family Restaurant is always so prosperous that there is not a single empty table in the dining hall at night.

Those who are mindful in business cannot help but covet the money that Wu Family Restaurant earns every year. Small restaurants in the same industry often cannot compete with Wu Family Restaurant due to their short capital. It seems that Wu Family Restaurant has become the only restaurant in Xuzhen. With Wu Family Restaurant, it seems that there cannot be a second restaurant. Not to mention anything else, whether they are residents of this town or travelers from afar, if they have a banquet, they must go to Wu Family Restaurant. It seems that inviting guests to Wu Family Restaurant is a very honorable thing. No matter how expensive the dishes are at Wu Family Restaurant, or how unremarkable the cooking is, they don't care. Xuzhen is densely populated and has a hub of vehicles and boats. It is also a large town in Jiangnan, but apart from Wu Family Restaurant, there is indeed no second decent restaurant. It is also strange that under the prestige of Wu Family Restaurant, no large restaurants have ever appeared, so the business of Wu Family Restaurant can almost be regarded as monopolized.

Wu Family Restaurant has always maintained its reputation.

But this year, several out-of-town merchants gathered a large amount of capital and planned to open another large restaurant in the town. The decoration of the shop and the equipment were all imitating Wu Family Restaurant. In terms of cooking, they specially processed it, setting prices with restraint. They were preparing to compete with Wu Family Restaurant, so they named the shop "Hu Family Restaurant."

As soon as Hu Family Restaurant opened, the business was unexpectedly good. This phenomenon not only surprised the owner of Wu Family Restaurant, but also surprised the people in the town. Hu Family Restaurant has been open for half a year, and people are saying:

"Wu Family Restaurant is finished. The former Wu Family Restaurant has become the current Hu Family Restaurant..."

Strange, Hu Family Restaurant is like a large magnet, attracting many customers. The old customers of Wu Family Restaurant in the past are like fallen leaves in a storm, blown to Hu Family Restaurant one by one. In this way, the century-old signboard of Wu Family Restaurant has lost its former reputation in the sharpened business competition.

The business of Wu Family Restaurant became quieter day by day...

The shop owner sat at the counter, smoking his cigarette, with nothing to do. Before, sitting at the counter, opening bills, managing money, and writing accounts, he was so busy that he didn't even have time to eat dinner for a few days. The six waiters hired in the dining hall were constantly walking back and forth, busy shouting for their parents. The two cooks, after cooking this dish, immediately cooked that one, only feeling that they couldn't keep up. But now, only two waiters are hired, but they are still idle.

"We must compete with Hu Family Restaurant!"

The owner of Wu Family Restaurant decided to compete with Hu Family Restaurant, so he posted advertisements everywhere, saying that from a certain date to a certain date, there would be a cheap sale for two weeks. After the advertisement was posted, the business did improve, and many old customers who had not traded for a long time also came. The owner felt happy, willing to sacrifice the capital to compete with Hu Family Restaurant. But after the two weeks of cheap sales passed, the business immediately returned to quiet, and, next to the advertisement of Wu Family Restaurant, the new advertisement of Hu Family Restaurant was clearly discovered, which read:

"Big cheap sale for a month!"

So the business of Hu Family Restaurant, following the victory of the competition, became more and more prosperous day by day. …

Banian Port 298

— Shuang'er

The newly established Banian Port, like a child playing with soap bubbles during the rubber price boom, was blown up and showed brilliant colors; but when the rubber price fell, it shrunk tightly, like a soap bubble suddenly bursting in the air.

At the center of the confluence of the Banian River and the Mira River, some scattered small houses with white walls and red tiles can be seen floating in the dense green forest from a distance, like a relief painting. Its two arms stretched out are the dark green forests, which look like a beautiful scene in the river. As the boat approached the shore of Banian Port, a red building of the oil company and a recessed small dock were revealed in the long Dutch imperial typeface, followed by a long plank bridge extending into the river, and some shop toilets arranged on the riverbed in the posture of police sentry boxes. On the rising tide, yellow feces mixed with tree stumps and leaves floated on the water, while Malay boatmen squeezed between steamers and small steamboats, swaying on the rapid tide.

Landing from a solid plank bridge in front of the customs, passing in front of the county government office, the post and telegraph office, the colonial barracks, and the local prison, Banian Port stretches out with a long road. Behind this lively street, several roads lead to quiet and charming places where white, Chinese, and Malay people's homes are built. No cars were seen, but bicycles rolled quickly under the feet of vigorous Malay people and lively Chinese youths. An unusual silence enveloped the location of this county government. (When I first entered this day from the turbid Singapore, I doubted my ears and eyes; but I finally accepted the feeling given to me by this new world with a sweet mood.) Only at the two ends of this street, the students of the Dutch and Chinese schools recited their books loudly, spreading out with the air current, like playing a subtle melody for this silent universe.

"Ten years ago, the Chinese merchants and wealthy Malay masters in this place used to fill their sacks with banknotes. From the distant forests, Chinese merchants, relying on bare feet swollen with water, squeezed rubber to this estuary to 'load' onto ships, and would fill bags full of gold. — Now, it is not easy to find a fifty-guilder bill." Captain told me when I landed, and shook his head sighing.

A Xing抢着接下去: "At that time, the shop assistants and coolies drank brandy every day, gambled mahjong for fifty guilders, and bought a pound of pork worth eight corners: now, —— the ghosts kill them·—— they can't afford to gamble mahjong for a guilder, and the butcher refuses to kill an extra pig. —— Be careful, they only eat beef once a week, and soon they won't be able to afford vegetables." After saying that, he lowered his head, dreaming of his old golden dreams.

The prosperity of Banian has really become a thing of the past, or in the future, will mankind create another prosperous face for this place! What remains now on this gray pier, and what weighs on the hearts of the poor people, is only a ruthless Dutch county magistrate and his secretary, a fierce-looking Dutch soldier" and his Javanese soldiers, a diligent government tax collector, and a puppet Banian King, as well as a Captain who started with five hundred yuan of capital, doing the work of maintaining the wreckage!

This is: four white people, one yellow people, and one brown race, are jointly building everything in the current Banian Port.

Leaving Puzhuang 299

— Shen Shengshi

By chance, I came to teach in such a small town for three months; the semester is over, and I will leave in a hurry, just as I came in a hurry.

There are no bizarre feelings to say about the short three-month town life. There, I discovered a deeper loneliness and desolation of life, and at the same time, I saw the poverty of the countryside and the panic and embarrassment of the residents in the face of the lake bandits' shooting; but who should pay attention to the voices of those farmers complaining about the age?

Although in the twilight, I often had the opportunity to enjoy another kind of consumption. My neighbor's residence was the home of the owner of a large rice shop. In the evening, they always opened their chatterbox, and God gave me a little chance to enjoy myself, listening to Mei Lanfang's signature plays and the peach blossom river song with trembling and nauseating voices through the wall. At the same time, young daughters were echoing and singing, with laughter permeating the songs; in this realm, it makes you meditate on the faint red happy life unfolding in the rice.

On a drizzly and gloomy day, walking to the river bank, listening to the women on the small boats from Jiangbei doing small business, crying for lack of rice to cook.

After sunset, there are often travelers dragging their faltering steps and carrying packages on the riverbank on their way to night.

In front of some small shops, there are villagers with earthy faces talking about the lake bandits' snipers.

During my three-month stay in Puzhuang, my only observations were these few things; for the sake of life, I will leave this small town in a hurry. For the school and several kind friends, before leaving, I can't help but have a little nostalgia; but I will finally leave them silently, and in the vast world, I will embark on a long journey.

After leaving Puzhuang, I will soon pack my bags to go to Wan, and the harsh winter will slip past in my hurried journey! Soon it will be early spring; my only hope is to hear from my friends in the South! At that time, please send me the spring news from Jiangnan.

The Human World (8) 300

— Li Huiying

After this idea was aroused, all my energy escaped from the situation of the opium couch in the west room and the inquiry about business conditions. I wanted to try to inquire a little about her personal life.

Indeed, she can be said to be a bitter person. She told me about her difficult and bad experiences. I also knew that her mother was not only not her biological mother, but also not her stepmother.

Her age, like what I judged her to be, was seventeen years old. She was from Xin Dian, a village downstream of Harbin. Her family originally grew crops. During the great flood of the Songhua River in July 1932, her home was washed away, and she was washed to Harbin. The person who led her here was her cousin. She repeatedly said that she would find a way to save her cousin from her predicament, and she also believed that her cousin was her only relative. Unexpectedly, this great person coveted sixty Harbin dollars, forgot her affection, and sent her to this place, and also found this young mother for her. She changed her clothes, cut her braids, and became a fashionable girl in the city. Life went on like this. However, she could not help but often miss her old hometown and her biological parents and brothers. Especially when a violent and incomparable guest mercilessly ravaged her body, it made her recall the past. The abyss of sin-filled city was gradually swallowing her weak girl.

She had no concept of the country, nor did she want to struggle for life. She only wished to die early and end her wishes. She did not blame heaven and did not blame the earth. She only blamed her bad fate, and the flood was precisely the life-threatening ghost who drove her to hell and into the grave.

When I told her that the flood was caused by the XX people, who deliberately dug the dikes to drown the anti-Japanese volunteers in the downstream area, the tension in her situation and the degree of her resentment were simply indescribable to me. I can say that she was a hundred times more nervous than when she fled the flood. She kept angrily shouting:

"Is that so? Is that so? Is that how it is! Is that how it is!"

Her hands were clenched tightly, and she looked like she was going to find the XX people to fight.

Really, how many people know that the flood was caused by the XX people? If it weren't for a person who dug the dikes with his own hands, he told me, how could I not think it was a natural disaster!

A burst of laughter came from the west room, probably because my friend had displayed his "male" power. I heard him shouting loudly:

"No way! You have to have a kiss!"

Why ask her for a kiss! I was just thinking this when there was no movement in the west room. Suddenly, Xiao Ju stretched out her hands and tightly held my hands, her body trembling as if she was cold, like a begging little bird. I looked at her for a while and saw that she had been attacked by some kind of terror. A moment ago, she was still telling me about her life. I also forgot that this situation was a little embarrassing for me, and my face didn't turn red. I was just thinking, who is she afraid of? It stands to reason that there are no strangers in this hut except me, so why is she afraid of me? That's not right, if she was afraid of me, she wouldn't be close to me. I was wrong to think of her that way.

Talks

Translation Year and Creation Year 301

— Qin Lv

I read an article by someone in the New Year's issue of "Literature," saying "I wish this year to be the year of translation following the year of magazines."

I think; before China has produced greater works, hoping this year to be a "year of creation" is more meaningful in every aspect than a "year of translation."

The difficulty of cultivating translation talents is more than ten times that of creation talents; the separation of languages of various countries, the inability to use them skillfully and instinctively, is of course an obstacle; however, the biggest reason is not here. It must be known that the task of translating literary works is not only to turn foreign languages into formal native languages. What is more important is to explore the depths of the original author's soul with one's own cultivation, grasp the formation of his thoughts when writing, and then purify it into my writing; only then can it become a true translation. In this kind of translation, the original author and the translator have merged into one.

How different are the worldviews of each person? Using individual and different cognition to translate the same work, even if you get "sweating profusely," the true breath does not exist. What remains is nothing more than some corpse-filled resurrected corpses. As for those who do not understand the meaning of the full text and borrow a dictionary to translate sentence by sentence, it goes without saying!

It is not without reason that there are few complete translations on the market.

The poverty of the Chinese literary world is not limited to translation; creation is not so! Instead of doing "thankless" translation work, why not work a little harder on creation in the near future? Perhaps the harvest of creation is more and more valuable than translation.

Efforts in creation have two meanings:

1. Effort in quality: A Cultivate a sound worldview. (Authenticity of the work.) (Content conditions.) B Develop fresh themes. C Use mature techniques. (Expressiveness of the work.) (Formal conditions.)

2. Effort in quantity: A Eliminate the Yuan Zhonglang school, the Public Security school, the Jingling school, the antique writing, and all kinds of non-donkey and non-horse miscellaneous essays. (Passive work) B Promote new talents and encourage the production of long works.

I hope that the year of creation, which is not just an empty shout, will come.

Chronicle of a Certain Year 302

— Hua Zhi

"Young master, the train is broken!"

I was jolted awake from my sleep by the shouting: It was Li Ma. Her small feet seemed hardly able to support her obese body as she swayed unsteadily in front of my mosquito net. Her voice sounded as if it were muffled by something, turning into a rough, guttural sound. Seeing that I was awake and just looking at her, she shouted:

"Young master, the train has been roaring all night, didn't you hear it? The city is completely overrun with 'ash worms' [soldiers]; they grab people when they see them. A'yun was almost dragged away when she went to buy vegetables; she lost her vegetable basket and scale. At the small bridgehead, the Gui Sheng family had their door pried open by 'ash worms,' and the father and son were so scared that they jumped into the back river and fled. Now, they're loitering in front of our door. A'yun has piled up the stone mortar and millstone to block the door..." She raised her fat palm in a gesture, "Young master, I want to go home, I'll be dragged away by the 'ash worms' and made into cannon fodder!"

Before I could answer, she stomped heavily down the stairs.

According to the newspapers these past few days, our county town, due to its railway connections, would sooner or later be drawn into the war front. The increased train traffic in the middle of the night didn't just start last night. Those in the city with some wealth had already sought refuge elsewhere. Li Ma wasn't aware of this. Otherwise, she would have cried to go home as soon as she heard about the war. Perhaps she is already safely home today, spared from being frightened. However, I was speculating why the trains would stop after the troops arrived. Isn't this a huge contradiction in military terms?

I went downstairs, and A'yun and Li Ma were both sitting blankly in the hall, like two molded clay figures. Li Ma, clutching her bundle of clothes, said with a mournful face:

"Young master, one can't even walk on the street anymore!"

"Really, they grab people when they see them," A'yun also said, "I saw it with my own eyes!"

Ignoring their words, I peered out through the gap in the door blocked by the stone mortar and millstone. The street was indeed deserted. Across the street, the door of the Gui Sheng family's house was wide open, and someone who looked like a local was carrying out a load of cabbage from their house.

"Local ruffians are the most terrifying," I thought to myself, "Before the soldiers loot everything, our own people are already carting things away."

The person was slowly approaching. Seeing the worn-out felt hat pressed down to his eyebrows, I was stunned. Wasn't that Gui Sheng? Frantically, I moved the stone mortar and millstone away and opened the door to call out to him.

"Young master, the soldiers have arrived."

He stopped the cabbage load, greeting me as if saying "Good day."

"Li Ma said the 'ash worms' pried open your door, and you jumped into the river and ran away?"

"No, that's not it." He shook his head with a smile, "Last night, for some reason, more than three thousand soldiers suddenly arrived. The temples and schools in the city have all been requisitioned for the troops. Today, they need people to cook, so they're grabbing anyone carrying a vegetable basket. I heard they're paying four small silver coins a day. Just now, two 'ash worms' passed by here. They saw the vegetable garden by the bridge and came to knock on my door to ask. They're willing to pay two dollars a load, which is the best business I've had all year. Young master, I'm

Page 20

sending it into the city, I'll be back later."

I watched Gui Sheng leave, then turned around. A'yun and Li Ma were standing behind me, their faces already wearing smiles. Knowing that they had heard Gui Sheng's words, I asked Li Ma:

"Do you still want to go home?"

She ran back inside, embarrassed. I told A'yun to dig up some vegetables from the garden to make a meal, and I headed to the city.

On the main street, all the shops were closed. The streets were full of soldiers in gray uniforms. If there were any locals, they were helping to carry things. I squeezed into the teahouse I frequented. Besides a few old regulars, it was completely occupied by soldiers. The tea master, Gen Fu, barely nodded to a soldier, trying to strike up a conversation. As I went to use my more or less fluent Northern [dialect] the soldier poured me a cup of tea instead and told me kindly: The front line is very victorious, but the × Yang Bridge was bombed the day before yesterday. Our superiors have deemed it prudent to use your land as a defensive line. There will be no changes within a few days. It is said that the retreat is slow and your land cannot be made a large line丨 More than 3,000 of our brothers have come and there is no place to cook!

Finally, he asked me with a smile: "Are you afraid?"

"What's there to be afraid of if there's no fighting!" They all laughed at what I said.

Big Sale 303

— San Duo

Opening a shop, hoping for customers to come, to turn a profit by turning over goods—this simple principle is something everyone knows. So, they put up large advertisements saying "Big Sale," but what they're really telling you is that their profit margins are a bit thinner during these three weeks. Customers are naturally eager for bargains. Two cigarette shops often compete fiercely over a single copper coin difference in the market price. Although there's an element of rivalry involved, it's ultimately for business reasons. I remember that when a "Big Sale" advertisement was posted in the past, customers from other places would come from afar to purchase goods. The annual seasonal sales and the once-a-year ×th anniversary sales were often very profitable for most shops. This is the principle of "small profits, large sales." Both the shops and the customers benefit. In the past two years, ordinary "Big Sales" have lost their original appeal. So, they're resorting to mutual promotions like "buy one get one free," "half price," and using prize coupons with large prizes like cars to maintain business. "Big Sales" are almost held year-round. However, looking at Shanghai's largest department stores, there are still very few customers. We don't ask whether their prices are at a loss or whether they're making even thinner profits. With such extensive advertising, "business" isn't improving. The reason isn't the business itself, but the obvious decline in customers' purchasing power. Then, spinning around desperately on the "Big Sale" carousel, how can they maintain this near-bankruptcy situation!

Fog 304

— Jing Jia

Fog is beautiful!

Waking up in the morning, I saw a white expanse outside the window, suspecting it was raining. Opening the window, I found it was a milky white fog, covering the entire field, obscuring everything.

After washing my face, I felt bored, so I moved a chair to the window, holding a cup of hot tea in both hands, sipping and watching the beautiful fog, almost forgetting myself.

After a while, the thick fog gradually thinned, and houses and trees closer by could be vaguely seen. People walking in the fog looked as if they were in the clouds. If I didn't feel the warmth of the teacup in my hands, I would have really suspected that I was living in the clouds.

Soon, the fog thinned a bit more, and things further away could also be distinguished. The trees in the distance only showed their tops, clustered together, like islands. At that moment, the gentle sunlight shone in, adding a layer of red to the milky white fog. The exposed treetops in the distance were also draped in golden yellow robes, sparkling like the cheeks of a graceful young woman, yet also like a shattered mirror.

After a while, the fog completely dissipated, and the sky was a lovely azure blue, the fields as clear and moving as if they had been scrubbed clean.

Fog is beautiful!
