Supplement to the Shenbao Newspaper Movie Special

Alice Faye Discusses the Many Temptations of Hollywood (Part 2) 312

— Xue Mei

The above are all the temptations outside the studio. However, there are still many temptations directly related to the work of filmmaking. Once you get an opportunity, whether it is as an extra, a small role, or after receiving a small contract,

Film work has a special requirement for actors: being punctual. In Hollywood, everyone working in the film industry must adhere to the rule of "early to bed, early to rise." However, there are many temptations there that constantly urge you to break that rule. You must know that chorus girls can sleep later, so staying up late is not a big deal, but that is not possible for film actors. Because film actors must get up at 6:30 am, or 7:00 am at the latest. After they get up, they have to do their hair and makeup, which takes a lot of time, while the filming work starts as early as 8:30 am or 9:00 am.

People working in the film studio need at least eight hours of sleep every day. If you reach a relatively important position and have to perform or film facial expressions, you must have abundant energy to perform vividly and be full of spirit. Only sufficient sleep can provide that. In front of the camera, even a little bit of fatigue will show. But even if you do not have an important position and do not have many facial expressions to make, eight hours of sleep is especially necessary, because you must always show your spirit, whether in front of the camera or when dealing with people, so that everyone in the studio, whether it is the producer, director, cinematographer, or other workers, has a good impression of you.

The eyes of the cinematographer are the sharpest. One look at your face and he knows if you are filming well or not. His sharp eyes have already seen whether you went out to play last night, whether you stayed up late, or whether you had insomnia. Therefore, no matter what, you must find a way to get eight hours of full sleep before 6:00 am. That means you must go to bed at 10:00 pm. Of course, sometimes staying up late is unavoidable. For example, shooting night scenes and testing films are all tasks that must be done at night. But you must always find ways to compensate for it. Otherwise, you will regret it in the future. But the temptation of Hollywood is precisely at play here. The sunlight of California does indeed have a special magic that makes people unwilling to stay indoors, but the nights and nightlife of California are equally tempting. Although Hollywood's nightlife is different from that of New York, without as many nightclubs as New York, the sheer number of social engagements in the film industry is considerable. They hold parties at home, in hotels, in bars, dance halls, theaters, etc., entertaining friends and colleagues, and it can be every night without exception.

Here, you need to understand that these stars who go out for social engagements are all in "Between pictures" – that is, in the rest period between finishing one film and starting the second. They use this break to wander around and socialize, but you are working or should be trying hard to find work, so how can you sacrifice yourself for others? You think that going to a social event for a while and sitting for a bit will allow you to come back, but once you get there, it is difficult to escape. If you do not have a strong will, you will end up losing the sleep you deserve. Soon, you will feel that these meaningless social engagements are not worthwhile. However, that is not what career-oriented Hollywood wants to force you to do. If you sit for a while, stand up and say, "I have an early call tomorrow, so I have to go first," they will understand and forgive you. Because they know that the work rules of the film studio emphasize time the most.

There is an even worse temptation, which is to watch movies every day. You often justify it to yourself: "This is for my own work." But soon, you will also suffer from sleep deprivation. Because if you leave the studio at 6:00 pm, have dinner, change clothes, and watch all the worthwhile films, you will not be able to go to bed at 10:00 pm. Working hard and diligently cannot be said to be a temptation in itself, but the most common danger for aspiring women who are new to Hollywood is working too much outside the studio and practicing too hard. You are often unwilling to give up your singing and dancing practice, and you often still practice language and drama. Of course, these are all necessary preparations for the future, but you must know how to limit yourself. As the saying goes, "Too much is as bad as too little." Good health is the foundation of everything.

In addition, there are many small temptations that actresses must avoid. First, do not be pretentious (outside the studio). Making every move as if you were an actress will be annoying to people everywhere. Hollywood is no exception. Also, after you have achieved some success, do not become conceited and arrogant. When you read the praise of you in the newspapers, you cannot think that you deserve it.

What Alice Faye said is of course very helpful to aspiring female stars who are new to Hollywood. But film practitioners in Shanghai may also wish to ponder it and take it as timely advice.

Film Reviews

Review of "Our Daily Bread" 313

— Ling He

Our Daily Bread丨Grand Theater

King Vidor, this great American writer, has already given people a deep impression from his past works. The most appropriate way to understand his style is to look at his life. He has experienced a difficult journey, and from his own life and the lives of his poor companions, he has realized the spirit of mutual assistance and great love between people. The characters appearing in his works are simple and honest good people. At the same time, the bad people he depicts are not absolutely bad, but rather caricatured.

In his works, one can usually appreciate a rich pastoral flavor, so he relatively believes that cities are always the root of evil. However, although the protagonists he creates are sometimes tempted by the harsh environment and go astray, King Vidor ultimately makes them rationally awaken.

Indeed, King Vidor is an idealist. This is because he has come into contact with many of the sorrows of the world, and he cannot help but express dissatisfaction with the real society. However, he cannot deeply understand the roots of social phenomena and only struggles against the evil society with his own self-confidence. Thus, he develops his humanity of mutual assistance and universal love, seeking ideal comfort from the cruel reality.

Regarding his past works, such as the silent film "The Crowd" and the sound films "The Big Parade" and "The Champ," they all consistently express the style described above. Now we must talk about the review of "Our Daily Bread," which he wrote himself.

Here, he takes the issue of unemployment as the theme and attempts to solve this serious social problem. Thus, he has a group of unemployed people reclaim wasteland. There are all kinds of unemployed people here, including artists and escaped prisoners. In this living group, they help each other, love each other, work together, eat together, and live together. They understand each other, blend with each other, and there is no such thing as hatred or grievances. It is even more clearly shown that although the male protagonist is temporarily tempted by money and women, abandoning his original wife and leaving the group, he soon realizes his mistake and works hard to participate in drought relief. Of course, his great ideal is fully expressed here. But his spirit, his great love, gives people great comfort, when people are experiencing extreme distress in reality. It is impossible for us to demand one hundred percent realism from King Vidor, but his sympathy for humanity is full in his works.

Furthermore, let us briefly observe what kind of techniques he used to complete his "Our Daily Bread." As someone who started as a studio laborer, his skilled use of production techniques is naturally flawless. For example, he absolutely does not use unnecessary gimmicks, but the merchant's attitude when the male protagonist exchanges a piano for a chicken is very funny, and the merchant's character is vividly depicted. Similarly, the scene in which the protagonist couple sleeps peacefully in the old farmhouse is very light and harmonious in its simple sketch. However, his strength does not lie here. The main thing is that he portrays the life of the group without any slackness. Especially after the male protagonist returns, it immediately builds to a climax. Whether in terms of musical effects or camera angles, it reaches a perfect state. As for the harmony of tones and the appropriate control of stillness and movement, he grasps the atmosphere before the male protagonist elopes with his lover and the unspoken sadness of the female protagonist very well. In short, this film deserves a higher evaluation.

Review of "The Life of Vergie Winters" 314

— You Jing

The Life of Vergie Winters 丨 Tai Shanghai Strait

This is an old-fashioned film about love above all else.

Louis Bromfield, the writer, makes us see in "The Life of Vergie Winters," whether in the selection of themes, the method of expression, or the worldview displayed by the creative attitude, is relatively conservative and old-fashioned.

He writes about Vergie Winters being slandered and unable to marry the person she loves, while John, who is from a "distinguished family," marries another woman named Laura. After the marriage, John resumes his old relationship with Vergie.

When John wants to divorce Laura and marry Vergie, she advises him to work hard for his future. During this time, Vergie gives birth to a daughter out of wedlock.

As time progresses, John's social status has become quite high, and Vergie's hatred also deepens. For the sake of love, she finally endures.

When her daughter grows up and also talks about love, Laura forces John to announce her origin. Thus, this tragedy unfolds.

John, who has achieved success, says that he can no longer "let this tragedy continue" and decisively wants to give Vergie the status of wife and mother. However, he is shot and killed by Laura, and Vergie is arrested, resulting in "this endless regret."

Here, the author, through Vergie's mouth, says to John: "I don't want anything but your love. I would rather live in the shadows of life." What more can we ask of an author with such a thorough love-only view?

The screenwriter may have been unable to escape the influence of the original work, and the whole play is rather scattered and dull. Especially the first half, from Vergie looking at John's funeral from the window of the prison and beginning to recall the past, until John participates in the election and Vergie gives birth to her daughter, this part is inevitably disorganized. The time expression from 1914 to 1932 is all done by inserting newspaper headlines, which is very monotonous. The repeated coming and going of the wealthy women buying hats also lacks variation.

Among the actors, Ann Harding is better. Her performance of a tragedy full of the bitterness of life is quite moving. John Boles, who plays John, should have had a great performance. Unfortunately, he did not achieve the results he should have.

Lido Theater to Open 315

The Spiritual Paradise in the Minds of Shanghai Citizens

Business starts at 9:15 PM on February 3rd

The newly built Lido Theater at the intersection of Guizhou Road and Beijing Road is scheduled to officially open at 9:15 PM on February 3rd. The theater was designed by the famous architect Fan Wenzhao. The building is magnificent and purely three-dimensional. The internal equipment, such as the Western Electric sound system, produces sound that is loud, clear, and subtly different. The projector uses a high-density current lamp, which is as bright as silver and does not show a yellow color. The orthophonic paper backing protects sound waves. This is a feature that is not yet commonly equipped in the largest theaters in the city. There is also a large hall upstairs for the audience to rest. It is comparable to the Grand Theater and the Nanjing Theater. The theater specializes in showing the second run of the best European and American films. The first films to be shown include MGM's honorary works of this year, "San Francisco" and "Tarzan and His Mate". The ticket prices are said to be 4, 6, and 8 jiao for daytime shows and 4, 7 jiao, and 1 yuan for evening shows. The illustration shows the exterior of the theater.

Movie Novel

The Legend of the Red Sheep Hero (Part 3) 316

— Zhao Chu

Feng Yunshan was giving a speech, and there were more than ten people listening. Brother Xu Er suddenly pushed the door open. Seeing Feng Yunshan, he quickly went forward and pulled him aside, whispering a few words. Feng's expression changed immediately upon hearing what he said, and he hurriedly told everyone to leave. He himself rushed to the Hong family to report the news. At this time, Hong Xiuquan and his wife, Lai, were standing side by side in the corridor, watching his younger sister, Hong Xuanjiao, practice martial arts. Suddenly, Feng Yunshan ran in breathlessly, shouting, "Is Brother Hong here?" Xuanjiao stopped her fist, and Xiuquan greeted him, asking what was the matter. Feng hurriedly said, "The county has already sent people to arrest us. Quickly think of a way to escape!" Hong was stunned and lost his mind. Feng urged him again, saying, "Hurry up, the people arresting us have already come out."

A group of ruthless yamen runners rushed straight to the entrance of the God Worshipping Society. No one answered when they knocked on the door. They broke down the door and found nothing. They shouted in unison, "Let's hurry to the Hong family to arrest them." Everyone swarmed over again. At this time, Hong Xiuquan, Feng Yunshan, Hong's wife, Lai, and Xuanjiao had already escaped. Lai and Xuanjiao changed into village women's attire, each carrying a package. Hong said to Lai and his sister, "Now you have to go to the countryside and hide for a few days. When we have a suitable place, we will send you a message." Lai held onto Xiuquan, wanting to say something. Xiuquan repeatedly said, "This is not the time to talk. Just listen to my message later." He then opened the small door in the back garden and walked out.

The yamen runners rushed in, searching each room without finding anyone. They then gathered in the courtyard. Then they caught an old servant. The old servant was frightened out of his wits. The yamen runners asked him where Hong Xiuquan was hiding. Tell them quickly. The old servant answered tremblingly, "Please spare me, sirs. I really don't know." The yamen runners were furious and punched him. At this time, a man ran in and reported, "I saw Hong Xiuquan and a man riding horses and escaping north." Everyone listened and chased after them like a swarm of bees. Let's say that Hong and Feng were riding on horseback, rushing quickly. Hong said, "Let's still go to Guangxi!" With that, the two whipped their horses, and in an instant they were gone. Fifteen or sixteen yamen runners, riding horses and carrying swords, rushed to the outskirts. They reined in their horses, looking around and discussing where to pursue. As a result, they split into two groups, searching in both directions. Hong and Feng saw pursuing soldiers behind them and whipped their horses even more. When they reached the river, they had to follow the river. A team of men had already detoured to meet them. Another team of men had also chased to the river and were also chasing along the riverbank. Hong and Feng, seeing pursuing soldiers in front and behind, were greatly alarmed. Suddenly, a clever idea came to him. Hong then said to Feng, "We only have this desperate plan to escape." With that, the two immediately dismounted, each whipping the horses behind them. The two horses ran away. The two threw their hats and boots into the river, and they themselves fled along the grassy riverbank. Before leaving, they threw a few large stones, creating turbulent water patterns on the river. Teams A and B met one after another. Someone had already seized the escaped horses of Hong and Feng, but could not find the two men. Later, someone saw the two men's hats and boots floating on the river. At that time, everyone was talking about it. Some people even picked up stones and threw them into the river to test the situation. As a result, the yamen runner said, "I'm afraid they were so anxious that they jumped into the river and died. We'll have to let it go." With that, everyone mounted their horses and returned dejectedly. Over here, Hong and Feng were secretly watching from the reeds. Feng said, "Today was really too dangerous! We almost fell into their hands." Hong Xiuquan, hearing this, sighed and said, "It's a pity they are also Han Chinese. Why do they have to force us to this point!" (To be continued)

Home
